Theory Diffie_Hellman

theory Diffie_Hellman
imports Cyclic_Group_SPMF Computational_Model
(* Title: Diffie_Hellman.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

section â€¹Specifying security using gamesâ€º

theory Diffie_Hellman imports
  CryptHOL.Cyclic_Group_SPMF
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
begin

subsection â€¹The DDH gameâ€º

locale ddh =
  fixes ğ’¢ :: "'grp cyclic_group" (structure)
begin

type_synonym 'grp' adversary = "'grp' â‡’ 'grp' â‡’ 'grp' â‡’ bool spmf"

definition ddh_0 :: "'grp adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where "ddh_0 ğ’œ = do {
     x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     ğ’œ (â™g [^] x) (â™g [^] y) (â™g [^] (x * y))
  }"

definition ddh_1 :: "'grp adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where "ddh_1 ğ’œ = do {
     x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     z â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     ğ’œ (â™g [^] x) (â™g [^] y) (â™g [^] z)
  }"

definition advantage :: "'grp adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (ddh_0 ğ’œ) True - spmf (ddh_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"

definition lossless :: "'grp adversary â‡’ bool"
where "lossless ğ’œ âŸ· (âˆ€Î± Î² Î³. lossless_spmf (ğ’œ Î± Î² Î³))"

lemma lossless_ddh_0:
  "âŸ¦ lossless ğ’œ; 0 < order ğ’¢ âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (ddh_0 ğ’œ)"
by(auto simp add: lossless_def ddh_0_def split_def Let_def)

lemma lossless_ddh_1:
  "âŸ¦ lossless ğ’œ; 0 < order ğ’¢ âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (ddh_1 ğ’œ)"
by(auto simp add: lossless_def ddh_1_def split_def Let_def)

end

subsection â€¹The LCDH gameâ€º

locale lcdh =
  fixes ğ’¢ :: "'grp cyclic_group" (structure)
begin

type_synonym 'grp' adversary = "'grp' â‡’ 'grp' â‡’ 'grp' set spmf"

definition lcdh :: "'grp adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where "lcdh ğ’œ = do { 
     x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     zs â† ğ’œ (â™g [^] x) (â™g [^] y);
     return_spmf (â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ zs)
  }"

definition advantage :: "'grp adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = spmf (lcdh ğ’œ) True"

definition lossless :: "'grp adversary â‡’ bool"
where "lossless ğ’œ âŸ· (âˆ€Î± Î². lossless_spmf (ğ’œ Î± Î²))"

lemma lossless_lcdh:
  "âŸ¦ lossless ğ’œ; 0 < order ğ’¢ âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (lcdh ğ’œ)"
by(auto simp add: lossless_def lcdh_def split_def Let_def)

end

end

Theory IND_CCA2

theory IND_CCA2
imports Computational_Model Negligible Environment_Functor
(* Title: IND_CCA2.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

theory IND_CCA2 imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  CryptHOL.Negligible
  CryptHOL.Environment_Functor
begin

locale pk_enc = 
  fixes key_gen :: "security â‡’ ('ekey Ã— 'dkey) spmf" â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and encrypt :: "security â‡’ 'ekey â‡’ 'plain â‡’ 'cipher spmf"  â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and decrypt :: "security â‡’ 'dkey â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ 'plain option" â€• â€¹deterministic, but not usedâ€º
  and valid_plain :: "security â‡’ 'plain â‡’ bool" â€• â€¹checks whether a plain text is valid, i.e., has the right formatâ€º

subsection â€¹The IND-CCA2 game for public-key encryptionâ€º

text â€¹
  We model an IND-CCA2 security game in the multi-user setting as described in
  \cite{BellareBoldyrevaMicali2000EUROCRYPT}.
â€º

locale ind_cca2 = pk_enc +
  constrains key_gen :: "security â‡’ ('ekey Ã— 'dkey) spmf"
  and encrypt :: "security â‡’ 'ekey â‡’ 'plain â‡’ 'cipher spmf"
  and decrypt :: "security â‡’ 'dkey â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ 'plain option"
  and valid_plain :: "security â‡’ 'plain â‡’ bool"
begin

type_synonym ('ekey', 'dkey', 'cipher') state_oracle = "('ekey' Ã— 'dkey' Ã— 'cipher' list) option"

fun decrypt_oracle
  :: "security â‡’ ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle â‡’ 'cipher
  â‡’ ('plain option Ã— ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle) spmf"
where
  "decrypt_oracle Î· None cipher = return_spmf (None, None)"
| "decrypt_oracle Î· (Some (ekey, dkey, cstars)) cipher = return_spmf
   (if cipher âˆˆ set cstars then None else decrypt Î· dkey cipher, Some (ekey, dkey, cstars))"

fun ekey_oracle
  :: "security â‡’ ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle â‡’ unit â‡’ ('ekey Ã— ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle) spmf"
where
  "ekey_oracle Î· None _ = do {
      (ekey, dkey) â† key_gen Î·;
      return_spmf (ekey, Some (ekey, dkey, []))
    }"
| "ekey_oracle Î· (Some (ekey, rest)) _ = return_spmf (ekey, Some (ekey, rest))"

lemma ekey_oracle_conv:
  "ekey_oracle Î· Ïƒ x =
  (case Ïƒ of None â‡’ map_spmf (Î»(ekey, dkey). (ekey, Some (ekey, dkey, []))) (key_gen Î·) 
   | Some (ekey, rest) â‡’ return_spmf (ekey, Some (ekey, rest)))"
by(cases Ïƒ)(auto simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf split_def)

context notes bind_spmf_cong[fundef_cong] begin
function encrypt_oracle
  :: "bool â‡’ security â‡’ ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle â‡’ 'plain Ã— 'plain
  â‡’ ('cipher Ã— ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle) spmf"
where
  "encrypt_oracle b Î· None m01 = do { (_, Ïƒ) â† ekey_oracle Î· None (); encrypt_oracle b Î· Ïƒ m01 }"
| "encrypt_oracle b Î· (Some (ekey, dkey, cstars)) (m0, m1) =
  (if valid_plain Î· m0 âˆ§ valid_plain Î· m1 then do {  
     let pb = (if b then m0 else m1);
     cstar â† encrypt Î· ekey pb;
     return_spmf (cstar, Some (ekey, dkey, cstar # cstars))
   } else return_pmf None)"
by pat_completeness auto
termination by(relation "Wellfounded.measure (Î»(b, Î·, Ïƒ, m01). case Ïƒ of None â‡’ 1 | _ â‡’ 0)") auto
end

subsubsection â€¹Single-user settingâ€º

type_synonym ('plain', 'cipher') callâ‡©1 = "unit + 'cipher' + 'plain' Ã— 'plain'"
type_synonym ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') retâ‡©1 = "'ekey' + 'plain' option + 'cipher'"

definition oracleâ‡©1 :: "bool â‡’ security 
  â‡’ (('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle, ('plain, 'cipher) callâ‡©1, ('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) retâ‡©1) oracle'"
where "oracleâ‡©1 b Î· = ekey_oracle Î· âŠ•â‡©O (decrypt_oracle Î· âŠ•â‡©O encrypt_oracle b Î·)"

lemma oracleâ‡©1_simps [simp]:
  "oracleâ‡©1 b Î· s (Inl x) = map_spmf (apfst Inl) (ekey_oracle Î· s x)"
  "oracleâ‡©1 b Î· s (Inr (Inl y)) = map_spmf (apfst (Inr âˆ˜ Inl)) (decrypt_oracle Î· s y)"
  "oracleâ‡©1 b Î· s (Inr (Inr z)) = map_spmf (apfst (Inr âˆ˜ Inr)) (encrypt_oracle b Î· s z)"
by(simp_all add: oracleâ‡©1_def spmf.map_comp apfst_compose o_def)

type_synonym ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©1' = 
  "(bool, ('plain', 'cipher') callâ‡©1, ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') retâ‡©1) gpv"
type_synonym ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©1 =
  "security â‡’ ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©1'"

definition ind_cca2â‡©1 :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1 â‡’ security â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "ind_cca2â‡©1 ğ’œ Î· = TRY do {
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (guess, s) â† exec_gpv (oracleâ‡©1 b Î·) (ğ’œ Î·) None;
    return_spmf (guess = b)
  } ELSE coin_spmf"

definition advantageâ‡©1 :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1 â‡’ advantage"
where "advantageâ‡©1 ğ’œ Î· = Â¦spmf (ind_cca2â‡©1 ğ’œ Î·) True - 1/2Â¦"

lemma advantageâ‡©1_nonneg: "advantageâ‡©1 ğ’œ Î· â‰¥ 0" by(simp add: advantageâ‡©1_def)

abbreviation secure_forâ‡©1 :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1 â‡’ bool"
where "secure_forâ‡©1 ğ’œ â‰¡ negligible (advantageâ‡©1 ğ’œ)"

definition ibounded_byâ‡©1' :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1' â‡’ nat â‡’ bool"
where "ibounded_byâ‡©1' ğ’œ q = interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ q"

abbreviation ibounded_byâ‡©1 :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1 â‡’ (security â‡’ nat) â‡’ bool"
where "ibounded_byâ‡©1 â‰¡ rel_envir ibounded_byâ‡©1'"

definition losslessâ‡©1' :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1' â‡’ bool"
where "losslessâ‡©1' ğ’œ = lossless_gpv â„_full ğ’œ"

abbreviation losslessâ‡©1 :: "('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©1 â‡’ bool"
where "losslessâ‡©1 â‰¡ pred_envir losslessâ‡©1'"

lemma lossless_decrypt_oracle [simp]: "lossless_spmf (decrypt_oracle Î· Ïƒ cipher)"
by(cases "(Î·, Ïƒ, cipher)" rule: decrypt_oracle.cases) simp_all

lemma lossless_ekey_oracle [simp]:
  "lossless_spmf (ekey_oracle Î· Ïƒ x) âŸ· (Ïƒ = None âŸ¶ lossless_spmf (key_gen Î·))"
by(cases "(Î·, Ïƒ, x)" rule: ekey_oracle.cases)(auto)

lemma lossless_encrypt_oracle [simp]:
  "âŸ¦ Ïƒ = None âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (key_gen Î·);
    â‹€ekey m. valid_plain Î· m âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (encrypt Î· ekey m) âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (encrypt_oracle b Î· Ïƒ (m0, m1)) âŸ· valid_plain Î· m0 âˆ§ valid_plain Î· m1"
apply(cases "(b, Î·, Ïƒ, (m0, m1))" rule: encrypt_oracle.cases)
apply(auto simp add: split_beta dest: lossless_spmfD_set_spmf_nonempty split: if_split_asm)
done

subsubsection â€¹Multi-user settingâ€º

definition oracleâ‡©n :: "bool â‡’ security
   â‡’ ('i â‡’ ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle, 'i Ã— ('plain, 'cipher) callâ‡©1, ('ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) retâ‡©1) oracle'"
where "oracleâ‡©n b Î· = family_oracle (Î»_. oracleâ‡©1 b Î·)"

lemma oracleâ‡©n_apply [simp]:
  "oracleâ‡©n b Î· s (i, x) = map_spmf (apsnd (fun_upd s i)) (oracleâ‡©1 b Î· (s i) x)"
by(simp add: oracleâ‡©n_def)

type_synonym ('i, 'ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©n' = 
  "(bool, 'i Ã— ('plain', 'cipher') callâ‡©1, ('ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') retâ‡©1) gpv"
type_synonym ('i, 'ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©n =
  "security â‡’ ('i, 'ekey', 'plain', 'cipher') adversaryâ‡©n'"

definition ind_cca2â‡©n :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n â‡’ security â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "ind_cca2â‡©n ğ’œ Î· = TRY do {
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (guess, Ïƒ) â† exec_gpv (oracleâ‡©n b Î·) (ğ’œ Î·) (Î»_. None);
    return_spmf (guess = b)
  } ELSE coin_spmf"

definition advantageâ‡©n :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n â‡’ advantage"
where "advantageâ‡©n ğ’œ Î· = Â¦spmf (ind_cca2â‡©n ğ’œ Î·) True - 1/2Â¦"

lemma advantageâ‡©n_nonneg: "advantageâ‡©n ğ’œ Î· â‰¥ 0" by(simp add: advantageâ‡©n_def)

abbreviation secure_forâ‡©n :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n â‡’ bool"
where "secure_forâ‡©n ğ’œ â‰¡ negligible (advantageâ‡©n ğ’œ)"

definition ibounded_byâ‡©n' :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n' â‡’ nat â‡’ bool"
where "ibounded_byâ‡©n' ğ’œ q = interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ q"

abbreviation ibounded_byâ‡©n :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n â‡’ (security â‡’ nat) â‡’ bool"
where "ibounded_byâ‡©n â‰¡ rel_envir ibounded_byâ‡©n'"

definition losslessâ‡©n' :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n' â‡’ bool"
where "losslessâ‡©n' ğ’œ = lossless_gpv â„_full ğ’œ"

abbreviation losslessâ‡©n :: "('i, 'ekey, 'plain, 'cipher) adversaryâ‡©n â‡’ bool"
where "losslessâ‡©n â‰¡ pred_envir losslessâ‡©n'"


definition cipher_queries :: "('i â‡’ ('ekey, 'dkey, 'cipher) state_oracle) â‡’ 'cipher set"
where "cipher_queries ose = (â‹ƒ(_, _, ciphers)âˆˆran ose. set ciphers)"

lemma cipher_queriesI:
  "âŸ¦ ose n = Some (ek, dk, ciphers); x âˆˆ set ciphers âŸ§ âŸ¹ x âˆˆ cipher_queries ose"
by(auto simp add: cipher_queries_def ran_def)

lemma cipher_queriesE:
  assumes "x âˆˆ cipher_queries ose"
  obtains (cipher_queries) n ek dk ciphers where "ose n = Some (ek, dk, ciphers)" "x âˆˆ set ciphers"
using assms by(auto simp add: cipher_queries_def ran_def)

lemma cipher_queries_updE:
  assumes "x âˆˆ cipher_queries (ose(n â†¦ (ek, dk, ciphers)))"
  obtains (old) "x âˆˆ cipher_queries ose" "x âˆ‰ set ciphers" | (new) "x âˆˆ set ciphers"
using assms by(cases "x âˆˆ set ciphers")(fastforce elim!: cipher_queriesE split: if_split_asm intro: cipher_queriesI)+

lemma cipher_queries_empty [simp]: "cipher_queries Map.empty = {}"
by(simp add: cipher_queries_def)

end

end

Theory IND_CCA2_sym

theory IND_CCA2_sym
imports Computational_Model
(* Title: IND_CCA2_sym.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich 
  Author: S. Reza Sefidgar, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹The IND-CCA2 security for symmetric encryption schemesâ€º

theory IND_CCA2_sym imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
begin

locale ind_cca =
  fixes key_gen :: "'key spmf"
  and encrypt :: "'key â‡’ 'message â‡’ 'cipher spmf"
  and decrypt :: "'key â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ 'message option"
  and msg_predicate :: "'message â‡’ bool"
begin

type_synonym ('message', 'cipher') adversary = 
  "(bool, 'message' Ã— 'message' + 'cipher', 'cipher' option + 'message' option) gpv"

definition oracle_encrypt :: "'key â‡’ bool â‡’ ('message Ã— 'message, 'cipher option, 'cipher set) callee"
where
  "oracle_encrypt k b L = (Î»(msg1, msg0).
     (case msg_predicate msg1 âˆ§ msg_predicate msg0 of
        True â‡’ do {
         c â† encrypt k (if b then msg1 else msg0);
         return_spmf (Some c, {c} âˆª L)
        }
     | False â‡’ return_spmf (None, L)))"

lemma lossless_oracle_encrypt [simp]:
  assumes "lossless_spmf (encrypt k m1)" and "lossless_spmf (encrypt k m0)"
  shows "lossless_spmf (oracle_encrypt k b L (m1, m0))"
using assms by (simp add: oracle_encrypt_def split: bool.split)

definition oracle_decrypt :: "'key â‡’ ('cipher, 'message option, 'cipher set) callee"
where "oracle_decrypt k L c = return_spmf (if c âˆˆ L then None else decrypt k c, L)"

lemma lossless_oracle_decrypt [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_decrypt k L c)"
by(simp add: oracle_decrypt_def)

definition game :: "('message, 'cipher) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game ğ’œ = do {
    key â† key_gen;
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (b', L') â† exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt key) ğ’œ {};
    return_spmf (b = b')
  }"

definition advantage :: "('message, 'cipher) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (game ğ’œ) True - 1 / 2Â¦"

lemma advantage_nonneg: "0 â‰¤ advantage ğ’œ" by(simp add: advantage_def)

end

end

Theory IND_CPA

theory IND_CPA
imports Computational_Model Negligible
(* Title: IND_CPA.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

theory IND_CPA imports
  CryptHOL.Generative_Probabilistic_Value
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  CryptHOL.Negligible
begin

subsection â€¹The IND-CPA game for symmetric encryption schemesâ€º

locale ind_cpa = 
  fixes key_gen :: "'key spmf" â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and encrypt :: "'key â‡’ 'plain â‡’ 'cipher spmf"  â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and decrypt :: "'key â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ 'plain option" â€• â€¹deterministic, but not usedâ€º
  and valid_plain :: "'plain â‡’ bool" â€• â€¹checks whether a plain text is valid, i.e., has the right formatâ€º
begin

text â€¹
  We cannot incorporate the predicate @{term valid_plain} in the type @{typ "'plain"} of plaintexts,
  because the single @{typ "'plain"} must contain plaintexts for all values of the security parameter,
  as HOL does not have dependent types.  Consequently, the oracle has to ensure that the received
  plaintexts are valid.
â€º

type_synonym ('plain', 'cipher', 'state) adversary = 
  "(('plain' Ã— 'plain') Ã— 'state, 'plain', 'cipher') gpv
   Ã— ('cipher' â‡’ 'state â‡’ (bool, 'plain', 'cipher') gpv)"

definition encrypt_oracle :: "'key â‡’ unit â‡’ 'plain â‡’ ('cipher Ã— unit) spmf"
where
  "encrypt_oracle key Ïƒ plain = do {
     cipher â† encrypt key plain;
     return_spmf (cipher, ())
  }"

definition ind_cpa :: "('plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "ind_cpa ğ’œ = do {
     let (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) = ğ’œ;
     key â† key_gen;
     b â† coin_spmf;
     (guess, _) â† exec_gpv (encrypt_oracle key) (do {
         ((m0, m1), Ïƒ) â† ğ’œ1;
         if valid_plain m0 âˆ§ valid_plain m1 then do {
           cipher â† lift_spmf (encrypt key (if b then m0 else m1));
           ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ
         } else lift_spmf coin_spmf
       }) ();
     return_spmf (guess = b)
  }"

definition advantage :: "('plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (ind_cpa ğ’œ) True - 1/2Â¦"

lemma advantage_nonneg: "advantage ğ’œ â‰¥ 0" by(simp add: advantage_def)

definition ibounded_by :: "('plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ enat â‡’ bool"
where 
  "ibounded_by = (Î»(ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q. 
  (âˆƒq1 q2. interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ1 q1 âˆ§ (âˆ€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_any_bounded_by (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2) âˆ§ q1 + q2 â‰¤ q))"

lemma ibounded_byE [consumes 1, case_names ibounded_by, elim?]:
  assumes "ibounded_by (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q"
  obtains q1 q2
  where "q1 + q2 â‰¤ q"
  and "interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ1 q1"
  and "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_any_bounded_by (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2"
using assms by(auto simp add: ibounded_by_def)

lemma ibounded_byI [intro?]:
  "âŸ¦ interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ1 q1; â‹€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_any_bounded_by (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2; q1 + q2 â‰¤ q âŸ§
  âŸ¹ ibounded_by (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q"
by(auto simp add: ibounded_by_def)

definition lossless :: "('plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ bool"
where "lossless = (Î»(ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2). lossless_gpv â„_full ğ’œ1 âˆ§ (âˆ€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ)))"

end

end

Theory IND_CPA_PK

theory IND_CPA_PK
imports Computational_Model Negligible
(* Title: IND_CPA_PK.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

theory IND_CPA_PK imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  CryptHOL.Negligible
begin

subsection â€¹The IND-CPA game for public-key encryption with oracle accessâ€º

locale ind_cpa_pk = 
  fixes key_gen :: "('pubkey Ã— 'privkey, 'call, 'ret) gpv" â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and aencrypt :: "'pubkey â‡’ 'plain â‡’ ('cipher, 'call, 'ret) gpv"  â€• â€¹probabilistic w/ access to an oracleâ€º
  and adecrypt :: "'privkey â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ ('plain, 'call, 'ret) gpv" â€• â€¹not usedâ€º
  and valid_plains :: "'plain â‡’ 'plain â‡’ bool" â€• â€¹checks whether a pair of plaintexts is valid, i.e., they have the right formatâ€º
begin

text â€¹
  We cannot incorporate the predicate @{term valid_plain} in the type @{typ "'plain"} of plaintexts,
  because the single @{typ "'plain"} must contain plaintexts for all values of the security parameter,
  as HOL does not have dependent types.  Consequently, the game has to ensure that the received
  plaintexts are valid.
â€º

type_synonym ('pubkey', 'plain', 'cipher', 'call', 'ret', 'state) adversary = 
  "('pubkey' â‡’ (('plain' Ã— 'plain') Ã— 'state, 'call', 'ret') gpv)
   Ã— ('cipher' â‡’ 'state â‡’ (bool, 'call', 'ret') gpv)"

fun ind_cpa :: "('pubkey, 'plain, 'cipher, 'call, 'ret, 'state) adversary â‡’ (bool, 'call, 'ret) gpv"
where
  "ind_cpa (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) = TRY do {
     (pk, sk) â† key_gen;
     b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
     ((m0, m1), Ïƒ) â† (ğ’œ1 pk);
     assert_gpv (valid_plains m0 m1);
     cipher â† aencrypt pk (if b then m0 else m1);
     guess â† ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ; 
     Done (guess = b)
   } ELSE lift_spmf coin_spmf"

definition advantage :: "('Ïƒ â‡’ 'call â‡’ ('ret Ã— 'Ïƒ) spmf) â‡’ 'Ïƒ â‡’ ('pubkey, 'plain, 'cipher, 'call, 'ret, 'state) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage oracle Ïƒ ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (run_gpv oracle (ind_cpa ğ’œ) Ïƒ) True - 1/2Â¦"

lemma advantage_nonneg: "advantage oracle Ïƒ ğ’œ â‰¥ 0" by(simp add: advantage_def)

definition ibounded_by :: "('call â‡’ bool) â‡’ ('pubkey, 'plain, 'cipher, 'call, 'ret, 'state) adversary â‡’ enat â‡’ bool"
where 
  "ibounded_by consider = (Î»(ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q. 
  (âˆƒq1 q2. (âˆ€pk. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ1 pk) q1) âˆ§ (âˆ€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2) âˆ§ q1 + q2 â‰¤ q))"

lemma ibounded_by'E [consumes 1, case_names ibounded_by', elim?]:
  assumes "ibounded_by consider (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q"
  obtains q1 q2
  where "q1 + q2 â‰¤ q"
  and "â‹€pk. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ1 pk) q1"
  and "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2"
using assms by(auto simp add: ibounded_by_def)

lemma ibounded_byI [intro?]:
  "âŸ¦ â‹€pk. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ1 pk) q1; â‹€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_bounded_by consider (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2; q1 + q2 â‰¤ q âŸ§
  âŸ¹ ibounded_by consider (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) q"
by(auto simp add: ibounded_by_def)

definition lossless :: "('pubkey, 'plain, 'cipher, 'call, 'ret, 'state) adversary â‡’ bool"
where "lossless = (Î»(ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2). (âˆ€pk. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ1 pk)) âˆ§ (âˆ€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ)))"

end

end

Theory IND_CPA_PK_Single

theory IND_CPA_PK_Single
imports Computational_Model
(* Title: IND_CPA_PK_Single.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

theory IND_CPA_PK_Single imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
begin

subsection â€¹The IND-CPA game (public key, single instance)â€º

locale ind_cpa = 
  fixes key_gen :: "('pub_key Ã— 'priv_key) spmf" â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and aencrypt :: "'pub_key â‡’ 'plain â‡’ 'cipher spmf"  â€• â€¹probabilisticâ€º
  and adecrypt :: "'priv_key â‡’ 'cipher â‡’ 'plain option" â€• â€¹deterministic, but not usedâ€º
  and valid_plains :: "'plain â‡’ 'plain â‡’ bool" â€• â€¹checks whether a pair of plaintexts is valid, i.e., they both have the right formatâ€º
begin

text â€¹
  We cannot incorporate the predicate @{term valid_plain} in the type @{typ "'plain"} of plaintexts,
  because the single @{typ "'plain"} must contain plaintexts for all values of the security parameter,
  as HOL does not have dependent types.  Consequently, the oracle has to ensure that the received
  plaintexts are valid.
â€º

type_synonym ('pub_key', 'plain', 'cipher', 'state) adversary = 
  "('pub_key' â‡’ (('plain' Ã— 'plain') Ã— 'state) spmf)
   Ã— ('cipher' â‡’ 'state â‡’ bool spmf)"

primrec ind_cpa :: "('pub_key, 'plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "ind_cpa (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) = TRY do {
     (pk, sk) â† key_gen;
     ((m0, m1), Ïƒ) â† ğ’œ1 pk;
     _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains m0 m1);
     b â† coin_spmf;
     cipher â† aencrypt pk (if b then m0 else m1);
     b' â† ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ;
     return_spmf (b = b')
  } ELSE coin_spmf"

declare ind_cpa.simps [simp del]

definition advantage :: "('pub_key, 'plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (ind_cpa ğ’œ) True - 1/2Â¦"

definition lossless :: "('pub_key, 'plain, 'cipher, 'state) adversary â‡’ bool"
where
  "lossless ğ’œ âŸ·
   ((âˆ€pk. lossless_spmf (fst ğ’œ pk)) âˆ§
        (âˆ€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_spmf (snd ğ’œ cipher Ïƒ)))"

lemma lossless_ind_cpa:
  "âŸ¦ lossless ğ’œ; lossless_spmf (key_gen) âŸ§ âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (ind_cpa ğ’œ)"
by(auto simp add: lossless_def ind_cpa_def split_def Let_def)

end

end

Theory SUF_CMA

theory SUF_CMA

theory SUF_CMA imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  CryptHOL.Negligible
  CryptHOL.Environment_Functor
begin

subsection â€¹Strongly existentially unforgeable signature schemeâ€º

locale sig_scheme =
  fixes key_gen :: "security â‡’ ('vkey Ã— 'sigkey) spmf"
  and sign :: "security â‡’ 'sigkey â‡’ 'message â‡’ 'signature spmf"
  and verify :: "security â‡’ 'vkey â‡’ 'message â‡’ 'signature â‡’ bool" â€• â€¹verification is deterministicâ€º
  and valid_message :: "security â‡’ 'message â‡’ bool"

locale suf_cma = sig_scheme +
  constrains key_gen :: "security â‡’ ('vkey Ã— 'sigkey) spmf"
  and sign :: "security â‡’ 'sigkey â‡’ 'message â‡’ 'signature spmf"
  and verify :: "security â‡’ 'vkey â‡’ 'message â‡’ 'signature â‡’ bool"
  and valid_message :: "security â‡’ 'message â‡’ bool"
begin

type_synonym ('vkey', 'sigkey', 'message', 'signature') state_oracle 
  = "('vkey' Ã— 'sigkey' Ã— ('message' Ã— 'signature') list) option"

fun vkey_oracle :: "security â‡’ (('vkey, 'sigkey, 'message, 'signature) state_oracle, unit, 'vkey) oracle'"
where
  "vkey_oracle Î· None _ = do {
     (vkey, sigkey) â† key_gen Î·;
     return_spmf (vkey, Some (vkey, sigkey, []))
   }"
| "â‹€log. vkey_oracle Î· (Some (vkey, sigkey, log)) _ = return_spmf (vkey, Some (vkey, sigkey, log))"

context notes bind_spmf_cong[fundef_cong] begin
function sign_oracle
  :: "security â‡’ (('vkey, 'sigkey, 'message, 'signature) state_oracle, 'message, 'signature) oracle'"
where
  "sign_oracle Î· None m = do { (_, Ïƒ) â† vkey_oracle Î· None (); sign_oracle Î· Ïƒ m }"
| "â‹€log. sign_oracle Î· (Some (vkey, skey, log)) m =
  (if valid_message Î· m then do {
    sig â† sign Î· skey m;
    return_spmf (sig, Some (vkey, skey, (m, sig) # log)) 
  } else return_pmf None)"
by pat_completeness auto
termination by(relation "Wellfounded.measure (Î»(Î·, Ïƒ, m). case Ïƒ of None â‡’ 1 | _ â‡’ 0)") auto
end

lemma lossless_vkey_oracle [simp]:
  "lossless_spmf (vkey_oracle Î· Ïƒ x) âŸ· (Ïƒ = None âŸ¶ lossless_spmf (key_gen Î·))"
by(cases "(Î·, Ïƒ, x)" rule: vkey_oracle.cases) auto

lemma lossless_sign_oracle [simp]:
  "âŸ¦ Ïƒ = None âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (key_gen Î·);
    â‹€skey m. valid_message Î· m âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (sign Î· skey m) âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (sign_oracle Î· Ïƒ m) âŸ· valid_message Î· m"
apply(cases "(Î·, Ïƒ, m)" rule: sign_oracle.cases)
apply(auto simp add: split_beta dest: lossless_spmfD_set_spmf_nonempty)
done

lemma lossless_sign_oracle_Some: fixes log shows
  "lossless_spmf (sign_oracle Î· (Some (vkey, skey, log)) m) âŸ· lossless_spmf (sign Î· skey m) âˆ§ valid_message Î· m"
by(simp)

subsubsection â€¹Single-user settingâ€º

type_synonym 'message' callâ‡©1 = "unit + 'message'"
type_synonym ('vkey', 'signature') retâ‡©1 = "'vkey' + 'signature'"

definition oracleâ‡©1 :: "security
  â‡’ (('vkey, 'sigkey, 'message, 'signature) state_oracle, 'message callâ‡©1, ('vkey, 'signature) retâ‡©1) oracle'"

Theory Pseudo_Random_Function

theory Pseudo_Random_Function
imports Computational_Model
(* Title: Pseudo_Random_Function.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

theory Pseudo_Random_Function imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
begin

subsection â€¹Pseudo-random functionâ€º

locale random_function =
  fixes p :: "'a spmf"
begin

type_synonym ('b,'a') dict = "'b â‡€ 'a'"

definition random_oracle :: "('b, 'a) dict â‡’ 'b â‡’ ('a Ã— ('b, 'a) dict) spmf"
where
  "random_oracle Ïƒ x =
  (case Ïƒ x of Some y â‡’ return_spmf (y, Ïƒ)
   | None â‡’ p â¤œ (Î»y. return_spmf (y, Ïƒ(x â†¦ y))))"

definition forgetful_random_oracle :: "unit â‡’ 'b â‡’ ('a Ã— unit) spmf"
where
  "forgetful_random_oracle Ïƒ x = p â¤œ (Î»y. return_spmf (y, ()))"

lemma weight_random_oracle [simp]:
  "weight_spmf p = 1 âŸ¹ weight_spmf (random_oracle Ïƒ x) = 1"
by(simp add: random_oracle_def weight_bind_spmf o_def split: option.split)

lemma lossless_random_oracle [simp]:
  "lossless_spmf p âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (random_oracle Ïƒ x)"
by(simp add: lossless_spmf_def)

sublocale finite: callee_invariant_on random_oracle "Î»Ïƒ. finite (dom Ïƒ)" â„_full
by(unfold_locales)(auto simp add: random_oracle_def split: option.splits)

lemma card_dom_random_oracle:
  assumes "interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ q"
  and "(y, Ïƒ') âˆˆ set_spmf (exec_gpv random_oracle ğ’œ Ïƒ)"
  and fin: "finite (dom Ïƒ)"
  shows "card (dom Ïƒ') â‰¤ q + card (dom Ïƒ)"
by(rule finite.interaction_bounded_by'_exec_gpv_count[OF assms(1-2)])
  (auto simp add: random_oracle_def fin card_insert_if simp del: fun_upd_apply split: option.split_asm)

end

subsection â€¹Pseudo-random functionâ€º

locale "prf" =
  fixes key_gen :: "'key spmf"
  and "prf" :: "'key â‡’ 'domain â‡’ 'range"
  and rand :: "'range spmf"
begin

sublocale random_function "rand" .

definition prf_oracle :: "'key â‡’ unit â‡’ 'domain â‡’ ('range Ã— unit) spmf"
where "prf_oracle key Ïƒ x = return_spmf (prf key x, ())"

type_synonym ('domain', 'range') adversary = "(bool, 'domain', 'range') gpv"

definition game_0 :: "('domain, 'range) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game_0 ğ’œ = do {
     key â† key_gen;
     (b, _) â† exec_gpv (prf_oracle key) ğ’œ ();
     return_spmf b
   }"

definition game_1 :: "('domain, 'range) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game_1 ğ’œ = do {
     (b, _) â† exec_gpv random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty;
     return_spmf b
   }"

definition advantage :: "('domain, 'range) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (game_0 ğ’œ) True - spmf (game_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"

lemma advantage_nonneg: "advantage ğ’œ â‰¥ 0"
by(simp add: advantage_def)

abbreviation lossless :: "('domain, 'range) adversary â‡’ bool"
where "lossless â‰¡ lossless_gpv â„_full"

abbreviation (input) ibounded_by :: "('domain, 'range) adversary â‡’ enat â‡’ bool"
where "ibounded_by â‰¡ interaction_any_bounded_by"

end

Theory Guessing_Many_One

theory Guessing_Many_One
imports Computational_Model GPV_Bisim
(* Title: Guessing_Many_One.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich 
  Author: S. Reza Sefidgar, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹Reducing games with many adversary guesses to games with single guessesâ€º

theory Guessing_Many_One imports
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  CryptHOL.GPV_Bisim
begin

locale guessing_many_one =
  fixes init :: "('c_o Ã— 'c_a Ã— 's) spmf"
  and "oracle" :: "'c_o â‡’ 's â‡’ 'call â‡’ ('ret Ã— 's) spmf"
  and "eval" :: "'c_o â‡’ 'c_a â‡’ 's â‡’ 'guess â‡’ bool spmf"
begin

type_synonym ('c_a', 'guess', 'call', 'ret') adversary_single = "'c_a' â‡’ ('guess', 'call', 'ret') gpv"

definition game_single :: "('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_single â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game_single ğ’œ = do {
    (c_o, c_a, s) â† init;
    (guess, s') â† exec_gpv (oracle c_o) (ğ’œ c_a) s;
    eval c_o c_a s' guess
  }"

definition advantage_single :: "('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_single â‡’ real"
where "advantage_single ğ’œ = spmf (game_single ğ’œ) True"


type_synonym ('c_a', 'guess', 'call', 'ret') adversary_many = "'c_a' â‡’ (unit, 'call' + 'guess', 'ret' + unit) gpv"

definition eval_oracle :: "'c_o â‡’ 'c_a â‡’ bool Ã— 's â‡’ 'guess â‡’ (unit Ã— (bool Ã— 's)) spmf"
where
  "eval_oracle c_o c_a = (Î»(b, s') guess. map_spmf (Î»b'. ((), (b âˆ¨ b', s'))) (eval c_o c_a s' guess))"

definition game_multi :: "('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_many â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game_multi ğ’œ = do {
     (c_o, c_a, s) â† init;
     (_, (b, _)) â† exec_gpv
       (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O eval_oracle c_o c_a)
       (ğ’œ c_a)
       (False, s);
     return_spmf b
  }"

definition advantage_multi :: "('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_many â‡’ real"
where "advantage_multi ğ’œ = spmf (game_multi ğ’œ) True"


type_synonym 'guess' reduction_state = "'guess' + nat"

primrec process_call :: "'guess reduction_state â‡’ 'call â‡’ ('ret option Ã— 'guess reduction_state, 'call, 'ret) gpv"
where
  "process_call (Inr j) x = do {
    ret â† Pause x Done;
    Done (Some ret, Inr j)
  }"
| "process_call (Inl guess) x = Done (None, Inl guess)"

primrec process_guess :: "'guess reduction_state â‡’ 'guess â‡’ (unit option Ã— 'guess reduction_state, 'call, 'ret) gpv"
where
  "process_guess (Inr j) guess = Done (if j > 0 then (Some (), Inr (j - 1)) else (None, Inl guess))"
| "process_guess (Inl guess) _ = Done (None, Inl guess)"

abbreviation reduction_oracle :: "'guess + nat â‡’ 'call + 'guess â‡’ (('ret + unit) option Ã— ('guess + nat), 'call, 'ret) gpv"
where "reduction_oracle â‰¡ plus_intercept_stop process_call process_guess"

definition reduction :: "nat â‡’ ('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_many â‡’ ('c_a, 'guess, 'call, 'ret) adversary_single"
where
  "reduction q ğ’œ c_a = do {
    j_star â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set {..<q});
    (_, s) â† inline_stop reduction_oracle (ğ’œ c_a) (Inr j_star);
    Done (projl s)
  }"

lemma many_single_reduction:
  assumes bound: "â‹€c_a c_o s. (c_o, c_a, s) âˆˆ set_spmf init âŸ¹ interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (ğ’œ c_a) q"
  and lossless_oracle: "â‹€c_a c_o s s' x. (c_o, c_a, s) âˆˆ set_spmf init âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (oracle c_o s' x)"
  and lossless_eval: "â‹€c_a c_o s s' guess. (c_o, c_a, s) âˆˆ set_spmf init âŸ¹ lossless_spmf (eval c_o c_a s' guess)"
  shows "advantage_multi ğ’œ â‰¤ advantage_single (reduction q ğ’œ) * q"
  including lifting_syntax
proof -
  define eval_oracle'
    where "eval_oracle' = (Î»c_o c_a ((id, occ :: nat option), s') guess. 
    map_spmf (Î»b'. case occ of Some jâ‡©0 â‡’ ((), (Suc id, Some jâ‡©0), s')
                                | None â‡’ ((), (Suc id, (if b' then Some id else None)), s'))
      (eval c_o c_a s' guess))"
  let ?multi'_body = "Î»c_o c_a s. exec_gpv (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O eval_oracle' c_o c_a) (ğ’œ c_a) ((0, None), s)"
  define game_multi' where "game_multi' = (Î»c_o c_a s. do {
    (_, ((id, jâ‡©0), s' :: 's)) â† ?multi'_body c_o c_a s;
    return_spmf (jâ‡©0 â‰  None) })"

  define initialize :: "('c_o â‡’ 'c_a â‡’ 's â‡’ nat â‡’ bool spmf) â‡’ bool spmf" where
    "initialize body = do {
      (c_o, c_a, s) â† init;
      jâ‡©s â† spmf_of_set {..<q};
      body c_o c_a s jâ‡©s }" for body
  define body2 where "body2 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s = do {
    (_, (id, jâ‡©0), s') â† ?multi'_body c_o c_a s;
    return_spmf (jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s) }" for c_o c_a s jâ‡©s
  let ?game2 = "initialize body2"

  define stop_oracle where "stop_oracle = (Î»c_o. 
     (Î»(idgs, s) x. case idgs of Inr _ â‡’ map_spmf (Î»(y, s). (Some y, (idgs, s))) (oracle c_o s x) | Inl _ â‡’ return_spmf (None, (idgs, s)))
     âŠ•â‡©Oâ‡§S
     (Î»(idgs, s) guess :: 'guess. return_spmf (case idgs of Inr 0 â‡’ (None, Inl (guess, s), s) | Inr (Suc i) â‡’ (Some (), Inr i, s) | Inl _ â‡’ (None, idgs, s))))"
  define body3 where "body3 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s = do {
    (_ :: unit option, idgs, _) â† exec_gpv_stop (stop_oracle c_o) (ğ’œ c_a) (Inr jâ‡©s, s);
    (b' :: bool) â† case idgs of Inr _ â‡’ return_spmf False | Inl (g, s') â‡’ eval c_o c_a s' g;
    return_spmf b' }" for c_o c_a s jâ‡©s
  let ?game3 = "initialize body3"

  { define S :: "bool â‡’ nat Ã— nat option â‡’ bool" where "S â‰¡ Î»b' (id, occ). b' âŸ· (âˆƒjâ‡©0. occ = Some jâ‡©0)"
    let ?S = "rel_prod S (=)"

    define initial :: "nat Ã— nat option" where "initial = (0, None)"
    define result :: "nat Ã— nat option â‡’ bool" where "result p = (snd p â‰  None)" for p
    have [transfer_rule]: "(S ===> (=)) (Î»b. b) result" by(simp add: rel_fun_def result_def S_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: "S False initial" by (simp add: S_def initial_def)

    have eval_oracle'[transfer_rule]: 
      "((=) ===> (=) ===> ?S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) ?S))
       eval_oracle eval_oracle'"
      unfolding eval_oracle_def[abs_def] eval_oracle'_def[abs_def]
      by (auto simp add: rel_fun_def S_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI split: option.split)
    
    have game_multi': "game_multi ğ’œ = bind_spmf init (Î»(c_o, c_a, s). game_multi' c_o c_a s)"
      unfolding game_multi_def game_multi'_def initial_def[symmetric]
      by (rewrite in "case_prod âŒ‘" in "bind_spmf _ (case_prod âŒ‘)" in "_ = bind_spmf _ âŒ‘" split_def)
         (fold result_def; transfer_prover) }
  moreover
  have "spmf (game_multi' c_o c_a s) True = spmf (bind_spmf (spmf_of_set {..<q}) (body2 c_o c_a s)) True * q"
    if "(c_o, c_a, s) âˆˆ set_spmf init" for c_o c_a s
  proof -
    have bnd: "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (ğ’œ c_a) q" using bound that by blast

    have bound_occ: "jâ‡©s < q" if that: "((), (id, Some jâ‡©s), s') âˆˆ set_spmf (?multi'_body c_o c_a s)" 
      for s' id jâ‡©s
    proof -
      have "id â‰¤ q" 
        by(rule oi_True.interaction_bounded_by'_exec_gpv_count[OF bnd that, where count="fst âˆ˜ fst", simplified])
          (auto simp add: eval_oracle'_def split: plus_oracle_split_asm option.split_asm)
      moreover let ?I = "Î»((id, occ), s'). case occ of None â‡’ True | Some jâ‡©s â‡’ jâ‡©s < id"
      have "callee_invariant (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O eval_oracle' c_o c_a) ?I"
        by(clarsimp simp add: split_def intro!: conjI[OF callee_invariant_extend_state_oracle_const'])
          (unfold_locales; auto simp add: eval_oracle'_def split: option.split_asm)
      from callee_invariant_on.exec_gpv_invariant[OF this that] have "jâ‡©s < id" by simp
      ultimately show ?thesis by simp
    qed

    let ?M = "measure (measure_spmf (?multi'_body c_o c_a s))"
    have "spmf (game_multi' c_o c_a s) True = ?M {(u, (id, jâ‡©0), s'). jâ‡©0 â‰  None}"
      by(auto simp add: game_multi'_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] split_def spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def)
    also have "{(u, (id, jâ‡©0), s'). jâ‡©0 â‰  None} =
      {((), (id, Some jâ‡©s), s') |jâ‡©s s' id. jâ‡©s < q} âˆª {((), (id, Some jâ‡©s), s') |jâ‡©s s' id. jâ‡©s â‰¥ q}"
      (is "_ = ?A âˆª _") by auto
    also have "?M â€¦ = ?M ?A"
      by (rule measure_spmf.measure_zero_union)(auto simp add: measure_spmf_zero_iff dest: bound_occ)
    also have "â€¦ = measure (measure_spmf (pair_spmf (spmf_of_set {..< q}) (?multi'_body c_o c_a s)))
         {(jâ‡©s, (), (id, jâ‡©0), s') |jâ‡©s jâ‡©0 s' id. jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s } * q"
      (is "_ = measure ?M' ?B * _")
    proof - 
      have "?B = {(jâ‡©s, (), (id, jâ‡©0), s') |jâ‡©s jâ‡©0 s' id. jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s âˆ§ jâ‡©s < q} âˆª
        {(jâ‡©s, (), (id, jâ‡©0), s') |jâ‡©s jâ‡©0 s' id. jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s âˆ§ jâ‡©s â‰¥ q}" (is "_ = ?Set1 âˆª ?Set2")
        by auto
      then have "measure ?M' ?B = measure ?M' (?Set1 âˆª ?Set2)" by simp
      also have "â€¦ = measure ?M' ?Set1"
        by (rule measure_spmf.measure_zero_union) (auto simp add: measure_spmf_zero_iff)
      also have "â€¦ = (âˆ‘jâˆˆ{0..<q}. measure ?M' ({j} Ã— {((), (id, Some j), s')|s' id. True}))"
        by(subst measure_spmf.finite_measure_finite_Union[symmetric])
          (auto intro!: arg_cong2[where f=measure] simp add: disjoint_family_on_def)
      also have "â€¦ = (âˆ‘jâˆˆ{0..<q}. 1 / q * measure (measure_spmf (?multi'_body c_o c_a s)) {((), (id, Some j), s')|s' id. True})"
        by(simp add: measure_pair_spmf_times spmf_conv_measure_spmf[symmetric] spmf_of_set)
      also have "â€¦ = 1 / q * measure (measure_spmf (?multi'_body c_o c_a s)) {((), (id, Some jâ‡©s), s')|jâ‡©s s' id. jâ‡©s < q}"
        unfolding sum_distrib_left[symmetric]
        by(subst measure_spmf.finite_measure_finite_Union[symmetric])
          (auto intro!: arg_cong2[where f=measure] simp add: disjoint_family_on_def)
      finally show ?thesis by simp
    qed
    also have "?B = (Î»(jâ‡©s, _, (_, jâ‡©0), _). jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s) -` {True}"
      by (auto simp add: vimage_def)
    also have rw2: "measure ?M' â€¦ = spmf (bind_spmf (spmf_of_set {..<q}) (body2 c_o c_a s)) True"
      by (simp add: body2_def[abs_def] measure_map_spmf[symmetric] map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf
        split_def pair_spmf_alt_def spmf_conv_measure_spmf[symmetric])
    finally show ?thesis .
  qed
  hence "spmf (bind_spmf init (Î»(c_a, c_o, s). game_multi' c_a c_o s)) True = spmf ?game2 True * q"
    unfolding initialize_def spmf_bind[where p=init]
    by (auto intro!: integral_cong_AE simp del: integral_mult_left_zero simp add: integral_mult_left_zero[symmetric])

  moreover
  have "ord_spmf (âŸ¶) (body2 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s) (body3 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s)"
    if init: "(c_o, c_a, s) âˆˆ set_spmf init" and jâ‡©s: "jâ‡©s < Suc q" for c_o c_a s jâ‡©s
  proof -
    define oracle2' where "oracle2' â‰¡ Î»(b, (id, gs), s) guess. if id = jâ‡©s then do {
        b' :: bool â† eval c_o c_a s guess;
        return_spmf ((), (Some b', (Suc id, Some (guess, s)), s))
      } else return_spmf ((), (b, (Suc id, gs), s))"

    let ?R = "Î»((id1, jâ‡©0), s1) (b', (id2, gs), s2). s1 = s2 âˆ§ id1 = id2 âˆ§ (jâ‡©0 = Some jâ‡©s âŸ¶ b' = Some True) âˆ§ (id2 â‰¤ jâ‡©s âŸ¶ b' = None)"
    from init have "rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) ?R)
      (exec_gpv (extend_state_oracle (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O eval_oracle' c_o c_a) (ğ’œ c_a) ((0, None), s))
      (exec_gpv (extend_state_oracle (extend_state_oracle (oracle c_o)) âŠ•â‡©O oracle2') (ğ’œ c_a) (None, (0, None), s))"
      by(intro exec_gpv_oracle_bisim[where X="?R"])(auto simp add: oracle2'_def eval_oracle'_def spmf_rel_map map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] rel_spmf_return_spmf2 lossless_eval o_def intro!: rel_spmf_reflI split: option.split_asm plus_oracle_split if_split_asm)
    then have "rel_spmf (âŸ¶) (body2 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s) 
      (do {
        (_, b', _, _) â† exec_gpv (â€ â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O oracle2') (ğ’œ c_a) (None, (0, None), s);
        return_spmf (b' = Some True) })"
      (is "rel_spmf _ _ ?body2'")
      â€• â€¹We do not get equality here because the right hand side may return @{const True} even
        when the bad event has happened before the @{text jâ‡©s}-th iteration.â€º
      unfolding body2_def by(rule rel_spmf_bindI) clarsimp
    also
    let ?guess_oracle = "Î»((id, gs), s) guess. return_spmf ((), (Suc id, if id = jâ‡©s then Some (guess, s) else gs), s)"
    let ?I = "Î»(idgs, s). case idgs of (_, None) â‡’ False | (i, Some _) â‡’ jâ‡©s < i"
    interpret I: callee_invariant_on "â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O ?guess_oracle" "?I" â„_full
      by(simp)(unfold_locales; auto split: option.split)

    let ?f = "Î»s. case snd (fst s) of None â‡’ return_spmf False | Some a â‡’ eval c_o c_a (snd a) (fst a)"
    let ?X = "Î»jâ‡©s (b1, (id1, gs1), s1) (b2, (id2, gs2), s2). b1 = b2 âˆ§ id1 = id2 âˆ§ gs1 = gs2 âˆ§ s1 = s2 âˆ§ (b2 = None âŸ· gs2 = None) âˆ§ (id2 â‰¤ jâ‡©s âŸ¶ b2 = None)"
    have "?body2' = do {
      (a, r, s) â† exec_gpv (Î»(r, s) x. do {
               (y, s') â† (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O ?guess_oracle) s x;
               if ?I s' âˆ§ r = None then map_spmf (Î»r. (y, Some r, s')) (?f s') else return_spmf (y, r, s')
             })
         (ğ’œ c_a) (None, (0, None), s);
      case r of None â‡’ ?f s â¤œ return_spmf | Some r' â‡’ return_spmf r' }"
      unfolding oracle2'_def spmf_rel_eq[symmetric]
      by(rule rel_spmf_bindI[OF exec_gpv_oracle_bisim'[where X="?X jâ‡©s"]])
        (auto simp add: bind_map_spmf o_def spmf.map_comp split_beta conj_comms map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] spmf_rel_map rel_spmf_reflI cong: conj_cong split: plus_oracle_split)
    also have "â€¦ = do {
        us' â† exec_gpv (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O ?guess_oracle) (ğ’œ c_a) ((0, None), s);
        (b' :: bool) â† ?f (snd us');
        return_spmf b' }"
      (is "_ = ?body2''")
      by(rule I.exec_gpv_bind_materialize[symmetric])(auto split: plus_oracle_split_asm option.split_asm)
    also have "â€¦ = do {
        us' â† exec_gpv_stop (lift_stop_oracle (â€ (oracle c_o) âŠ•â‡©O ?guess_oracle)) (ğ’œ c_a) ((0, None), s);
        (b' :: bool) â† ?f (snd us');
        return_spmf b' }"
      supply lift_stop_oracle_transfer[transfer_rule] gpv_stop_transfer[transfer_rule] exec_gpv_parametric'[transfer_rule]
      by transfer simp
    also let ?S = "Î»((id1, gs1), s1) ((id2, gs2), s2). gs1 = gs2 âˆ§ (gs2 = None âŸ¶ s1 = s2 âˆ§ id1 = id2) âˆ§ (gs1 = None âŸ· id1 â‰¤ jâ‡©s)"
    have "ord_spmf (âŸ¶) â€¦ (exec_gpv_stop ((Î»((id, gs), s) x. case gs of None â‡’ lift_stop_oracle (â€ (oracle c_o)) ((id, gs), s) x | Some _ â‡’ return_spmf (None, ((id, gs), s))) âŠ•â‡©Oâ‡§S
            (Î»((id, gs), s) guess. return_spmf (if id â‰¥ jâ‡©s then None else Some (), (Suc id, if id = jâ‡©s then Some (guess, s) else gs), s)))
           (ğ’œ c_a) ((0, None), s) â¤œ
          (Î»us'. case snd (fst (snd us')) of None â‡’ return_spmf False | Some a â‡’ eval c_o c_a (snd a) (fst a)))"
      unfolding body3_def stop_oracle_def
      by(rule ord_spmf_exec_gpv_stop[where stop = "Î»((id, guess), _). guess â‰  None" and S="?S", THEN ord_spmf_bindI])
        (auto split: prod.split_asm plus_oracle_split_asm split!: plus_oracle_stop_split simp del: not_None_eq simp add: spmf.map_comp o_def apfst_compose ord_spmf_map_spmf1 ord_spmf_map_spmf2 split_beta ord_spmf_return_spmf2 intro!: ord_spmf_reflI)
    also let ?X = "Î»((id, gs), s1) (idgs, s2). s1 = s2 âˆ§ (case (gs, idgs) of (None, Inr id') â‡’ id' = jâ‡©s - id âˆ§ id â‰¤ jâ‡©s | (Some gs, Inl gs') â‡’ gs = gs' âˆ§ id > jâ‡©s | _ â‡’ False)"
    have "â€¦ = body3 c_o c_a s jâ‡©s" unfolding body3_def spmf_rel_eq[symmetric] stop_oracle_def
      by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim'[where X="?X", THEN rel_spmf_bindI])
        (auto split: option.split_asm plus_oracle_stop_split nat.splits split!: sum.split simp add: spmf_rel_map intro!: rel_spmf_reflI)
    finally show ?thesis by(rule pmf.rel_mono_strong)(auto elim!: option.rel_cases ord_option.cases)
  qed
  { then have "ord_spmf (âŸ¶) ?game2 ?game3"
      by(clarsimp simp add: initialize_def intro!: ord_spmf_bind_reflI)
    also
    let ?X = "Î»(gsid, s) (gid, s'). s = s' âˆ§ rel_sum (Î»(g, s1) g'. g = g' âˆ§ s1 = s') (=) gsid gid"
    have "rel_spmf (âŸ¶) ?game3 (game_single (reduction q ğ’œ))"
      unfolding body3_def stop_oracle_def game_single_def reduction_def split_def initialize_def
      apply(clarsimp simp add: bind_map_spmf exec_gpv_bind exec_gpv_inline intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
      apply(rule rel_spmf_bindI[OF exec_gpv_oracle_bisim'[where X="?X"]])
      apply(auto split: plus_oracle_stop_split elim!: rel_sum.cases simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] split_def spmf_rel_map rel_spmf_reflI rel_spmf_return_spmf1 lossless_eval split: nat.split)
      done
    finally have "ord_spmf (âŸ¶) ?game2 (game_single (reduction q ğ’œ))"
      by(rule pmf.rel_mono_strong)(auto elim!: option.rel_cases ord_option.cases)
    from this[THEN ord_spmf_measureD, of "{True}"]
    have "spmf ?game2 True â‰¤ spmf (game_single (reduction q ğ’œ)) True" unfolding spmf_conv_measure_spmf
      by(rule ord_le_eq_trans)(auto intro: arg_cong2[where f=measure]) }
  ultimately show ?thesis unfolding advantage_multi_def advantage_single_def 
    by(simp add: mult_right_mono)
qed

end

end

Theory Unpredictable_Function

theory Unpredictable_Function
imports Guessing_Many_One
(* Title: Unpredictable_Function.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich 
  Author: S. Reza Sefidgar, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹Unpredictable functionâ€º

theory Unpredictable_Function imports
  Guessing_Many_One
begin

locale upf =
  fixes key_gen :: "'key spmf"
  and hash :: "'key â‡’ 'x â‡’ 'hash"
begin

type_synonym ('x', 'hash') adversary = "(unit, 'x' + ('x' Ã— 'hash'), 'hash' + unit) gpv"

definition oracle_hash :: "'key â‡’ ('x, 'hash, 'x set) callee"
where
  "oracle_hash k = (Î»L y. do {
    let t = hash k y;
    let L = insert y L;
    return_spmf (t, L)
  })"

definition oracle_flag :: "'key â‡’ ('x Ã— 'hash, unit, bool Ã— 'x set) callee"
where
  "oracle_flag = (Î»key (flg, L) (y, t).
    return_spmf ((), (flg âˆ¨ (t = (hash key y) âˆ§ y âˆ‰ L), L)))"

abbreviation "oracle" :: "'key â‡’ ('x + 'x Ã— 'hash, 'hash + unit, bool Ã— 'x set) callee"
where "oracle key â‰¡ â€ (oracle_hash key) âŠ•â‡©O oracle_flag key"

definition game :: "('x, 'hash) adversary â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game ğ’œ = do {
    key â† key_gen;
    (_, (flag', L')) â† exec_gpv (oracle key) ğ’œ (False, {});
    return_spmf flag'
  }"

definition advantage :: "('x, 'hash) adversary â‡’ real"
where "advantage ğ’œ = spmf (game ğ’œ) True"

type_synonym ('x', 'hash') adversary1 = "('x' Ã— 'hash', 'x', 'hash') gpv"

definition game1 :: "('x, 'hash) adversary1 â‡’ bool spmf"
where
  "game1 ğ’œ = do {
    key â† key_gen;
    ((m, h), L) â† exec_gpv (oracle_hash key) ğ’œ {};
    return_spmf (h = hash key m âˆ§ m âˆ‰ L)
  }"

definition advantage1 :: "('x, 'hash) adversary1 â‡’ real"
  where "advantage1 ğ’œ = spmf (game1 ğ’œ) True"

lemma advantage_advantage1:
  assumes bound: "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) ğ’œ q"
  shows "advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ advantage1 (guessing_many_one.reduction q (Î»_ :: unit. ğ’œ) ()) * q"
proof -
  let ?init = "map_spmf (Î»key. (key, (), {})) key_gen"
  let ?oracle = "Î»key . oracle_hash key"
  let ?eval = "Î»key (_ :: unit) L (x, h). return_spmf (h = hash key x âˆ§ x âˆ‰ L)"

  interpret guessing_many_one ?init ?oracle ?eval .

  have [simp]: "oracle_flag key = eval_oracle key ()" for key
    by(simp add: oracle_flag_def eval_oracle_def fun_eq_iff)
  have "game ğ’œ = game_multi (Î»_. ğ’œ)"
    by(auto simp add: game_multi_def game_def bind_map_spmf intro!: bind_spmf_cong[OF refl])
  hence "advantage ğ’œ = advantage_multi (Î»_. ğ’œ)" by(simp add: advantage_def advantage_multi_def)
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ advantage_single (reduction q (Î»_. ğ’œ)) * q" using bound
    by(rule many_single_reduction)(auto simp add: oracle_hash_def)
  also have "advantage_single (reduction q (Î»_. ğ’œ)) = advantage1 (reduction q (Î»_. ğ’œ) ())" for ğ’œ
    unfolding advantage1_def advantage_single_def
    by(auto simp add: game1_def game_single_def bind_map_spmf o_def intro!: bind_spmf_cong[OF refl] arg_cong2[where f=spmf])
  finally show ?thesis .
qed

end

end

Theory Elgamal

theory Elgamal
imports Diffie_Hellman IND_CPA_PK_Single Negligible
(* Title: Elgamal.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

section â€¹Cryptographic constructions and their securityâ€º

theory Elgamal imports
  CryptHOL.Cyclic_Group_SPMF
  CryptHOL.Computational_Model
  Diffie_Hellman
  IND_CPA_PK_Single
  CryptHOL.Negligible
begin

subsection â€¹Elgamal encryption schemeâ€º

locale elgamal_base =
  fixes ğ’¢ :: "'grp cyclic_group" (structure)
begin

type_synonym 'grp' pub_key = "'grp'"
type_synonym 'grp' priv_key = nat
type_synonym 'grp' plain = 'grp'
type_synonym 'grp' cipher = "'grp' Ã— 'grp'"

definition key_gen :: "('grp pub_key Ã— 'grp priv_key) spmf"
where 
  "key_gen = do {
     x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     return_spmf (â™g [^] x, x)
  }"

lemma key_gen_alt:
  "key_gen = map_spmf (Î»x. (â™g [^] x, x)) (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢))"
by(simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf key_gen_def)

definition aencrypt :: "'grp pub_key â‡’ 'grp â‡’ 'grp cipher spmf"
where
  "aencrypt Î± msg = do {
    y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
    return_spmf (â™g [^] y, (Î± [^] y) âŠ— msg)
  }"

lemma aencrypt_alt:
  "aencrypt Î± msg = map_spmf (Î»y. (â™g [^] y, (Î± [^] y) âŠ— msg)) (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢))"
by(simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf aencrypt_def)

definition adecrypt :: "'grp priv_key â‡’ 'grp cipher â‡’ 'grp option"
where
  "adecrypt x = (Î»(Î², Î¶). Some (Î¶ âŠ— (inv (Î² [^] x))))"

abbreviation valid_plains :: "'grp â‡’ 'grp â‡’ bool"
where "valid_plains msg1 msg2 â‰¡ msg1 âˆˆ carrier ğ’¢ âˆ§ msg2 âˆˆ carrier ğ’¢"

sublocale ind_cpa: ind_cpa key_gen aencrypt adecrypt valid_plains .
sublocale ddh: ddh ğ’¢ .

fun elgamal_adversary :: "('grp pub_key, 'grp plain, 'grp cipher, 'state) ind_cpa.adversary â‡’ 'grp ddh.adversary"
where
  "elgamal_adversary (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) Î± Î² Î³ = TRY do {
    b â† coin_spmf;
    ((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ) â† ğ’œ1 Î±;
    â€• â€¹have to check that the attacker actually sends two elements from the group; otherwise flip a coinâ€º
    _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
    guess â† ğ’œ2 (Î², Î³ âŠ— (if b then msg1 else msg2)) Ïƒ;
    return_spmf (guess = b)
  } ELSE coin_spmf"

end

locale elgamal = elgamal_base + cyclic_group ğ’¢
begin 

theorem advantage_elgamal: "ind_cpa.advantage ğ’œ = ddh.advantage (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
  including monad_normalisation
proof -
  obtain ğ’œ1 and ğ’œ2 where "ğ’œ = (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2)" by(cases ğ’œ)
  note [simp] = this order_gt_0_iff_finite finite_carrier try_spmf_bind_out split_def o_def spmf_of_set bind_map_spmf weight_spmf_le_1 scale_bind_spmf bind_spmf_const
    and [cong] = bind_spmf_cong_simp
  have "ddh.ddh_1 (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ) = TRY do {
       x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
       y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
       ((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ) â† ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x);
       _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
       b â† coin_spmf;
       z â† map_spmf (Î»z. â™g [^] z âŠ— (if b then msg1 else msg2)) (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢));
       guess â† ğ’œ2 (â™g [^] y, z) Ïƒ;
       return_spmf (guess âŸ· b)
     } ELSE coin_spmf"
    by(simp add: ddh.ddh_1_def)
  also have "â€¦ = TRY do {
       x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
       y â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
       ((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ) â† ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x);
       _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
       z â† map_spmf (Î»z. â™g [^] z) (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢));
       guess â† ğ’œ2 (â™g [^] y, z) Ïƒ;
       map_spmf ((=) guess) coin_spmf
     } ELSE coin_spmf"
    by(simp add: sample_uniform_one_time_pad map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[where p=coin_spmf])
  also have "â€¦ = coin_spmf"
    by(simp add: map_eq_const_coin_spmf try_bind_spmf_lossless2')
  also have "ddh.ddh_0 (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ) = ind_cpa.ind_cpa ğ’œ"
    by(simp add: ddh.ddh_0_def IND_CPA_PK_Single.ind_cpa.ind_cpa_def key_gen_def aencrypt_def nat_pow_pow eq_commute)
  ultimately show ?thesis by(simp add: ddh.advantage_def ind_cpa.advantage_def)
qed

end
  
locale elgamal_asymp = 
  fixes ğ’¢ :: "security â‡’ 'grp cyclic_group"
  assumes elgamal: "â‹€Î·. elgamal (ğ’¢ Î·)"
begin
  
sublocale elgamal "ğ’¢ Î·" for Î· by(simp add: elgamal)
    
theorem elgamal_secure:
  "negligible (Î»Î·. ind_cpa.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·))" if "negligible (Î»Î·. ddh.advantage Î· (elgamal_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)))"
  by(simp add: advantage_elgamal that)

end

context elgamal_base begin

lemma lossless_key_gen [simp]: "lossless_spmf (key_gen) âŸ· 0 < order ğ’¢"
by(simp add: key_gen_def Let_def)

lemma lossless_aencrypt [simp]:
  "lossless_spmf (aencrypt key plain) âŸ· 0 < order ğ’¢"
by(simp add: aencrypt_def Let_def)

  "âŸ¦ ind_cpa.lossless ğ’œ; 0 < order ğ’¢ âŸ§
  âŸ¹ ddh.lossless (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
by(cases ğ’œ)(simp add: ddh.lossless_def ind_cpa.lossless_def Let_def split_def)

end

end

Theory Hashed_Elgamal

theory Hashed_Elgamal
imports GPV_Bisim List_Bits IND_CPA_PK Diffie_Hellman
(* Title: Hashed_Elgamal.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹Hashed Elgamal in the Random Oracle Modelâ€º

theory Hashed_Elgamal imports
  CryptHOL.GPV_Bisim
  CryptHOL.Cyclic_Group_SPMF
  CryptHOL.List_Bits
  IND_CPA_PK
  Diffie_Hellman
begin

type_synonym bitstring = "bool list"

locale hash_oracle = fixes len :: "nat" begin

type_synonym 'a state = "'a â‡€ bitstring"

definition "oracle" :: "'a state â‡’ 'a â‡’ (bitstring Ã— 'a state) spmf"
where
  "oracle Ïƒ x = 
  (case Ïƒ x of None â‡’ do {
     bs â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len);
     return_spmf (bs, Ïƒ(x â†¦ bs))
   } | Some bs â‡’ return_spmf (bs, Ïƒ))"

abbreviation (input) initial :: "'a state" where "initial â‰¡ Map.empty"

inductive invariant :: "'a state â‡’ bool"
where
  invariant: "âŸ¦ finite (dom Ïƒ); length ` ran Ïƒ âŠ† {len} âŸ§ âŸ¹ invariant Ïƒ"

lemma invariant_initial [simp]: "invariant initial"
by(rule invariant.intros) auto

lemma invariant_update [simp]: "âŸ¦ invariant Ïƒ; length bs = len âŸ§ âŸ¹ invariant (Ïƒ(x â†¦ bs))"
by(auto simp add: invariant.simps ran_def)
                           
lemma invariant [intro!, simp]: "callee_invariant oracle invariant"
by unfold_locales(simp_all add: oracle_def in_nlists_UNIV split: option.split_asm)

lemma invariant_in_dom [simp]: "callee_invariant oracle (Î»Ïƒ. x âˆˆ dom Ïƒ)"
by unfold_locales(simp_all add: oracle_def split: option.split_asm)

lemma lossless_oracle [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle Ïƒ x)"
by(simp add: oracle_def split: option.split)

lemma card_dom_state:
  assumes Ïƒ': "(x, Ïƒ') âˆˆ set_spmf (exec_gpv oracle gpv Ïƒ)"
  and ibound: "interaction_any_bounded_by gpv n"
  shows "card (dom Ïƒ') â‰¤ n + card (dom Ïƒ)"
proof(cases "finite (dom Ïƒ)")
  case True
  interpret callee_invariant_on "oracle" "Î»Ïƒ. finite (dom Ïƒ)" â„_full
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: oracle_def split: option.split_asm)
  from ibound Ïƒ' _ _ _ True show ?thesis
    by(rule interaction_bounded_by'_exec_gpv_count)(auto simp add: oracle_def card_insert_if simp del: fun_upd_apply split: option.split_asm)
next
  case False
  interpret callee_invariant_on "oracle" "Î»Ïƒ'. dom Ïƒ âŠ† dom Ïƒ'" â„_full
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: oracle_def split: option.split_asm)
  from Ïƒ' have "dom Ïƒ âŠ† dom Ïƒ'" by(rule exec_gpv_invariant) simp_all
  with False have "infinite (dom Ïƒ')" by(auto intro: finite_subset)
  with False show ?thesis by simp
qed

end

locale elgamal_base =
  fixes ğ’¢ :: "'grp cyclic_group" (structure)
  and len_plain :: "nat"
begin

sublocale hash: hash_oracle "len_plain" .
abbreviation hash :: "'grp â‡’ (bitstring, 'grp, bitstring) gpv"
where "hash x â‰¡ Pause x Done"

type_synonym 'grp' pub_key = "'grp'"
type_synonym 'grp' priv_key = nat
type_synonym plain = bitstring
type_synonym 'grp' cipher = "'grp' Ã— bitstring"

definition key_gen :: "('grp pub_key Ã— 'grp priv_key) spmf"
where 
  "key_gen = do {
     x â† sample_uniform (order ğ’¢);
     return_spmf (â™g [^] x, x)
  }"

definition aencrypt :: "'grp pub_key â‡’ plain â‡’ ('grp cipher, 'grp, bitstring) gpv"
where
  "aencrypt Î± msg = do {
    y â† lift_spmf (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢));
    h â† hash (Î± [^] y);
    Done (â™g [^] y, h [âŠ•] msg)
  }"

definition adecrypt :: "'grp priv_key â‡’ 'grp cipher â‡’ (plain, 'grp, bitstring) gpv"
where
  "adecrypt x = (Î»(Î², Î¶). do {
    h â† hash (Î² [^] x);
    Done (Î¶ [âŠ•] h)
  })"

definition valid_plains :: "plain â‡’ plain â‡’ bool"
where "valid_plains msg1 msg2 âŸ· length msg1 = len_plain âˆ§ length msg2 = len_plain"

lemma lossless_aencrypt [simp]: "lossless_gpv â„ (aencrypt Î± msg) âŸ· 0 < order ğ’¢"
by(simp add: aencrypt_def Let_def)

lemma interaction_bounded_by_aencrypt [interaction_bound, simp]:
  "interaction_bounded_by (Î»_. True) (aencrypt Î± msg) 1"
unfolding aencrypt_def by interaction_bound(simp add: one_enat_def SUP_le_iff)

sublocale ind_cpa: ind_cpa_pk "lift_spmf key_gen" aencrypt adecrypt valid_plains .
sublocale lcdh: lcdh ğ’¢ .

fun elgamal_adversary
   :: "('grp pub_key, plain, 'grp cipher, 'grp, bitstring, 'state) ind_cpa.adversary
   â‡’ 'grp lcdh.adversary"                     
where
  "elgamal_adversary (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) Î± Î² = do {
    (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), s) â† exec_gpv hash.oracle (ğ’œ1 Î±) hash.initial;
    â€• â€¹have to check that the attacker actually sends an element from the group; otherwise stop earlyâ€º
    TRY do {
      _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
      h' â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain);
      (guess, s') â† exec_gpv hash.oracle (ğ’œ2 (Î², h') Ïƒ) s;
      return_spmf (dom s')
    } ELSE return_spmf (dom s)
  }"

end

locale elgamal = elgamal_base +
  assumes cyclic_group: "cyclic_group ğ’¢"
begin

interpretation cyclic_group ğ’¢ by(fact cyclic_group)

lemma advantage_elgamal: 
  includes lifting_syntax
  assumes lossless: "ind_cpa.lossless ğ’œ"
  shows "ind_cpa.advantage hash.oracle hash.initial ğ’œ â‰¤ lcdh.advantage (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
proof -
  note [cong del] = if_weak_cong and [split del] = if_split
    and [simp] = map_lift_spmf gpv.map_id lossless_weight_spmfD map_spmf_bind_spmf bind_spmf_const
  obtain ğ’œ1 ğ’œ2 where ğ’œ [simp]: "ğ’œ = (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2)" by(cases "ğ’œ")

  interpret cyclic_group: cyclic_group ğ’¢ by(rule cyclic_group)
  from finite_carrier have [simp]: "order ğ’¢ > 0" using order_gt_0_iff_finite by(simp)

  from lossless have lossless1 [simp]: "â‹€pk. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ1 pk)"
    and lossless2 [simp]: "â‹€Ïƒ cipher. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ2 Ïƒ cipher)"
    by(auto simp add: ind_cpa.lossless_def)

  text â€¹We change the adversary's oracle to record the queries made by the adversaryâ€º
  define hash_oracle' where "hash_oracle' = (Î»Ïƒ x. do {
      h â† hash x;
      Done (h, insert x Ïƒ)
    })"
  have [simp]: "lossless_gpv â„_full (hash_oracle' Ïƒ x)" for Ïƒ x by(simp add: hash_oracle'_def)
  have [simp]: "lossless_gpv â„_full (inline hash_oracle' (ğ’œ1 Î±) s)" for Î± s
    by(rule lossless_inline[where â„=â„_full]) simp_all
  define game0 where "game0 = TRY do {
      (pk, _) â† lift_spmf key_gen;
      b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
      (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), s) â† inline hash_oracle' (ğ’œ1 pk) {};
      assert_gpv (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
      cipher â† aencrypt pk (if b then msg1 else msg2);
      (guess, s') â† inline hash_oracle' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s;
      Done (guess = b)
    } ELSE lift_spmf coin_spmf"
  { define cr where "cr = (Î»_ :: unit. Î»_ :: 'a set. True)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "cr () {}" by(simp add: cr_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: "((=) ===> cr ===> cr) (Î»_ Ïƒ. Ïƒ) insert" by(simp add: rel_fun_def cr_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: "(cr ===> (=) ===> rel_gpv (rel_prod (=) cr) (=)) id_oracle hash_oracle'"
      unfolding hash_oracle'_def id_oracle_def[abs_def] bind_gpv_Pause bind_rpv_Done by transfer_prover
    have "ind_cpa.ind_cpa ğ’œ = game0" unfolding game0_def ğ’œ ind_cpa_pk.ind_cpa.simps
      by(transfer fixing: ğ’¢ len_plain ğ’œ1 ğ’œ2)(simp add: bind_map_gpv o_def ind_cpa_pk.ind_cpa.simps split_def) }
  note game0 = this
  have game0_alt_def: "game0 = do {
      x â† lift_spmf (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢));
      b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
      (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), s) â† inline hash_oracle' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) {};
      TRY do {
        _ :: unit â† assert_gpv (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
        cipher â† aencrypt (â™g [^] x) (if b then msg1 else msg2);
        (guess, s') â† inline hash_oracle' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s;
        Done (guess = b)
      } ELSE lift_spmf coin_spmf
    }"
    by(simp add: split_def game0_def key_gen_def lift_spmf_bind_spmf bind_gpv_assoc try_gpv_bind_lossless[symmetric])

  define hash_oracle'' where "hash_oracle'' = (Î»(s, Ïƒ) (x :: 'a). do {
      (h, Ïƒ') â† case Ïƒ x of
          None â‡’ bind_spmf (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain)) (Î»bs. return_spmf (bs, Ïƒ(x â†¦ bs)))
        | Some (bs :: bitstring) â‡’ return_spmf (bs, Ïƒ);
      return_spmf (h, insert x s, Ïƒ')
    })"
  have *: "exec_gpv hash.oracle (inline hash_oracle' ğ’œ s) Ïƒ = 
    map_spmf (Î»(a, b, c). ((a, b), c)) (exec_gpv hash_oracle'' ğ’œ (s, Ïƒ))" for ğ’œ Ïƒ s
    by(simp add: hash_oracle'_def hash_oracle''_def hash.oracle_def Let_def exec_gpv_inline exec_gpv_bind o_def split_def cong del: option.case_cong_weak)
  have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (hash_oracle'' s plain)" for s plain
    by(simp add: hash_oracle''_def Let_def split: prod.split option.split)
  have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ1 Î±) s)" for s Î±
    by(rule lossless_exec_gpv[where â„=â„_full]) simp_all
  have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ2 Ïƒ cipher) s)" for Ïƒ cipher s
    by(rule lossless_exec_gpv[where â„=â„_full]) simp_all

  let ?sample = "Î»f. bind_spmf (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢)) (Î»x. bind_spmf (sample_uniform (order ğ’¢)) (f x))"
  define game1 where "game1 = (Î»(x :: nat) (y :: nat). do {
      b â† coin_spmf;
      (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), (s, s_h)) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) ({}, hash.initial);
      TRY do {
        _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
        (h, s_h') â† hash.oracle s_h (â™g [^] (x * y));
        let cipher = (â™g [^] y, h [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg2));
        (guess, (s', s_h'')) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, s_h');
        return_spmf (guess = b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s')
      } ELSE do {
        b â† coin_spmf;
        return_spmf (b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s)
      }
    })"
  have game01: "run_gpv hash.oracle game0 hash.initial = map_spmf fst (?sample game1)"
    apply(simp add: exec_gpv_bind split_def bind_gpv_assoc aencrypt_def game0_alt_def game1_def o_def bind_map_spmf if_distribs * try_bind_assert_gpv try_bind_assert_spmf lossless_inline[where â„=â„_full] bind_rpv_def nat_pow_pow del: bind_spmf_const)
    including monad_normalisation by(simp add: bind_rpv_def nat_pow_pow)
  
  define game2 where "game2 = (Î»(x :: nat) (y :: nat). do {
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), (s, s_h)) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) ({}, hash.initial);
    TRY do {
      _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
      h â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain);
      â€• â€¹We do not do the lookup in â€¹s_hâ€º here, so the rest differs only if the adversary guessed â€¹yâ€ºâ€º
      let cipher = (â™g [^] y, h [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg2));
      (guess, (s', s_h')) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, s_h);
      return_spmf (guess = b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s')
    } ELSE do {
      b â† coin_spmf;
      return_spmf (b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s)
    }
  })"
  interpret inv'': callee_invariant_on "hash_oracle''" "Î»(s, s_h). s = dom s_h" â„_full
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: hash_oracle''_def split: option.split_asm if_split)
  have in_encrypt_oracle: "callee_invariant hash_oracle'' (Î»(s, _). x âˆˆ s)" for x
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: hash_oracle''_def)

  { fix x y :: nat
    let ?bad = "Î»(s, s_h). â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s"
    let ?X = "Î»(s, s_h) (s', s_h'). s = dom s_h âˆ§ s' = s âˆ§ s_h = s_h'(â™g [^] (x * y) := None)"
    have bisim:
      "rel_spmf (Î»(a, s1') (b, s2'). ?bad s1' = ?bad s2' âˆ§ (Â¬ ?bad s2' âŸ¶ a = b âˆ§ ?X s1' s2'))
             (hash_oracle'' s1 plain) (hash_oracle'' s2 plain)"
      if "?X s1 s2" for s1 s2 plain using that
      by(auto split: prod.splits intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI simp add: hash_oracle''_def rel_spmf_return_spmf2 fun_upd_twist split: option.split dest!: fun_upd_eqD)
    have inv: "callee_invariant hash_oracle'' ?bad"
      by(unfold_locales)(auto simp add: hash_oracle''_def split: option.split_asm)
    have "rel_spmf (Î»(win, bad) (win', bad'). bad = bad' âˆ§ (Â¬ bad' âŸ¶ win = win')) (game2 x y) (game1 x y)"
      unfolding game1_def game2_def
      apply(clarsimp simp add: split_def o_def hash.oracle_def rel_spmf_bind_reflI if_distribs intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI simp del: bind_spmf_const)
      apply(rule rel_spmf_try_spmf)
      subgoal for b msg1 msg2 Ïƒ s s_h
        apply(rule rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
        apply(drule inv''.exec_gpv_invariant; clarsimp)
        apply(cases "s_h (â™g [^] (x * y))")
        subgoal â€• â€¹case @{const None}â€º
          apply(clarsimp intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
          apply(rule rel_spmf_bindI)
           apply(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim_bad_full[OF _ _ bisim inv inv, where R="Î»(x, s1) (y, s2). ?bad s1 = ?bad s2 âˆ§ (Â¬ ?bad s2 âŸ¶ x = y)"]; clarsimp simp add: fun_upd_idem; fail)
          apply clarsimp
          done
        subgoal by(auto intro!: rel_spmf_bindI1 rel_spmf_bindI2 lossless_exec_gpv[where â„=â„_full] dest!: callee_invariant_on.exec_gpv_invariant[OF in_encrypt_oracle])
        done
      subgoal by(rule rel_spmf_reflI) simp
      done }
  hence "rel_spmf (Î»(win, bad) (win', bad'). (bad âŸ· bad') âˆ§ (Â¬ bad' âŸ¶ win âŸ· win')) (?sample game2) (?sample game1)"
    by(intro rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
  hence "Â¦measure (measure_spmf (?sample game2)) {(x, _). x} - measure (measure_spmf (?sample game1)) {(y, _). y}Â¦
        â‰¤ measure (measure_spmf (?sample game2)) {(_, bad). bad}"
    unfolding split_def by(rule fundamental_lemma)
  moreover have "measure (measure_spmf (?sample game2)) {(x, _). x} = spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game2)) True"
    and "measure (measure_spmf (?sample game1)) {(y, _). y} = spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game1)) True"
    and "measure (measure_spmf (?sample game2)) {(_, bad). bad} = spmf (map_spmf snd (?sample game2)) True"
    unfolding spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf by(rule arg_cong2[where f=measure]; fastforce)+
  ultimately have hop23: "Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game2)) True - spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game1)) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ spmf (map_spmf snd (?sample game2)) True" by simp

  define game3
    where "game3 = (Î»f :: _ â‡’ _ â‡’ _ â‡’ bitstring spmf â‡’ _ spmf. Î»(x :: nat) (y :: nat). do {
      b â† coin_spmf;
      (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), (s, s_h)) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) ({}, hash.initial);
      TRY do {
        _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
        h' â† f b msg1 msg2 (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain));
        let cipher = (â™g [^] y, h');
        (guess, (s', s_h')) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, s_h);
        return_spmf (guess = b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s')
      } ELSE do {
        b â† coin_spmf;
        return_spmf (b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ s)
      }
    })"
  let ?f = "Î»b msg1 msg2. map_spmf (Î»h. (if b then msg1 else msg2) [âŠ•] h)"
  have "game2 x y = game3 ?f x y" for x y
    unfolding game2_def game3_def by(simp add: Let_def bind_map_spmf xor_list_commute o_def nat_pow_pow)
  also have "game3 ?f x y = game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x) x y" for x y (* optimistic sampling *)
    unfolding game3_def
    by(auto intro!: try_spmf_cong bind_spmf_cong[OF refl] if_cong[OF refl] simp add: split_def one_time_pad valid_plains_def simp del: map_spmf_of_set_inj_on bind_spmf_const split: if_split)
  finally have game23: "game2 x y = game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x) x y" for x y .

  define hash_oracle''' where "hash_oracle''' = (Î»(Ïƒ :: 'a â‡’ _). hash.oracle Ïƒ)"
  { define bisim where "bisim = (Î»Ïƒ (s :: 'a set, Ïƒ' :: 'a â‡€ bitstring). s = dom Ïƒ âˆ§ Ïƒ = Ïƒ')"
    have [transfer_rule]: "bisim Map_empty ({}, Map_empty)" by(simp add: bisim_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: "(bisim ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) bisim)) hash_oracle''' hash_oracle''"
      by(auto simp add: hash_oracle''_def split_def hash_oracle'''_def spmf_rel_map hash.oracle_def rel_fun_def bisim_def split: option.split intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
    have * [transfer_rule]: "(bisim ===> (=)) dom fst" by(simp add: bisim_def rel_fun_def)
    have * [transfer_rule]: "(bisim ===> (=)) (Î»x. x) snd" by(simp add: rel_fun_def bisim_def)
    have "game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x) x y = do {
        b â† coin_spmf;
        (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), s) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle''' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) hash.initial;
        TRY do {
          _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
          h' â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain);
          let cipher = (â™g [^] y, h');
          (guess, s') â† exec_gpv hash_oracle''' (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s;
          return_spmf (guess = b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ dom s')
        } ELSE do {
          b â† coin_spmf;
          return_spmf (b, â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ dom s)
        }
      }" for x y
      unfolding game3_def Map_empty_def[symmetric] split_def fst_conv snd_conv prod.collapse
      by(transfer fixing: ğ’œ1 ğ’¢ len_plain x y ğ’œ2) simp
    moreover have "map_spmf snd (â€¦ x y) = do {
        zs â† elgamal_adversary ğ’œ (â™g [^] x) (â™g [^] y);
        return_spmf (â™g [^] (x * y) âˆˆ zs)
      }" for x y
      by(simp add: o_def split_def hash_oracle'''_def map_try_spmf map_scale_spmf)
        (simp add: o_def map_try_spmf map_scale_spmf map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] spmf.map_comp map_const_spmf_of_set)
    ultimately have "map_spmf snd (?sample (game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x))) = lcdh.lcdh (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
      by(simp add: o_def lcdh.lcdh_def Let_def nat_pow_pow) }
  then have game2_snd: "map_spmf snd (?sample game2) = lcdh.lcdh (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
    using game23 by(simp add: o_def)

  have "map_spmf fst (game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x) x y) = do {
      (((msg1, msg2), Ïƒ), (s, s_h)) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ1 (â™g [^] x)) ({}, hash.initial);
      TRY do {
        _ :: unit â† assert_spmf (valid_plains msg1 msg2);
        h' â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len_plain);
        (guess, (s', s_h')) â† exec_gpv hash_oracle'' (ğ’œ2 (â™g [^] y, h') Ïƒ) (s, s_h);
        map_spmf ((=) guess) coin_spmf
      } ELSE coin_spmf
    }" for x y 
    including monad_normalisation
    by(simp add: game3_def o_def split_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf try_spmf_bind_out weight_spmf_le_1 scale_bind_spmf try_spmf_bind_out1 bind_scale_spmf)
  then have game3_fst: "map_spmf fst (game3 (Î»_ _ _ x. x) x y) = coin_spmf" for x y
    by(simp add: o_def if_distribs spmf.map_comp map_eq_const_coin_spmf split_def)

  have "ind_cpa.advantage hash.oracle hash.initial ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game1)) True - 1 / 2Â¦"
    using game0 by(simp add: ind_cpa_pk.advantage_def game01 o_def)
  also have "â€¦ = Â¦1 / 2 - spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game1)) TrueÂ¦"
    by(simp add: abs_minus_commute)
  also have "1 / 2 = spmf (map_spmf fst (?sample game2)) True"
    by(simp add: game23 o_def game3_fst spmf_of_set)
  also note hop23 also note game2_snd
  finally show ?thesis by(simp add: lcdh.advantage_def)
qed

end

context elgamal_base begin

lemma lossless_key_gen [simp]: "lossless_spmf key_gen âŸ· 0 < order ğ’¢"
by(simp add: key_gen_def Let_def)

  "âŸ¦ ind_cpa.lossless ğ’œ; â‹€Î·. 0 < order ğ’¢ âŸ§
  âŸ¹ lcdh.lossless (elgamal_adversary ğ’œ)"
by(cases ğ’œ)(auto simp add: lcdh.lossless_def ind_cpa.lossless_def split_def Let_def intro!: lossless_exec_gpv[where â„=â„_full] lossless_inline)
