Theory RP_RF

theory RP_RF
imports Pseudo_Random_Function Pseudo_Random_Permutation GPV_Bisim
(* Title: RP_RF.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹The random-permutation random-function switching lemmaâ€º

theory RP_RF imports
  Pseudo_Random_Function
  Pseudo_Random_Permutation
  CryptHOL.GPV_Bisim
begin

lemma rp_resample:
  assumes "B âŠ† A âˆª C" "A âˆ© C = {}" "C âŠ† B" and finB: "finite B"
  shows "bind_spmf (spmf_of_set B) (Î»x. if x âˆˆ A then spmf_of_set C else return_spmf x) = spmf_of_set C"
proof(cases "C = {} âˆ¨ A âˆ© B = {}")
  case False
  define A' where "A' â‰¡ A âˆ© B"
  from False have C: "C â‰  {}" and A': "A' â‰  {}" by(auto simp add: A'_def)
  have B: "B = A' âˆª C" using assms by(auto simp add: A'_def)
  with finB have finA: "finite A'" and finC: "finite C" by simp_all
  from assms have A'C: "A' âˆ© C = {}" by(auto simp add: A'_def)
  have "bind_spmf (spmf_of_set B) (Î»x. if x âˆˆ A then spmf_of_set C else return_spmf x) = 
        bind_spmf (spmf_of_set B) (Î»x. if x âˆˆ A' then spmf_of_set C else return_spmf x)"
    by(rule bind_spmf_cong[OF refl])(simp add: set_spmf_of_set finB A'_def)
  also have "â€¦ = spmf_of_set C" (is "?lhs = ?rhs")
  proof(rule spmf_eqI)
    fix i
    have "(âˆ‘xâˆˆC. spmf (if x âˆˆ A' then spmf_of_set C else return_spmf x) i) = indicator C i" using finA finC 
      by(simp add: disjoint_notin1[OF A'C] indicator_single_Some sum_mult_indicator[of C "Î»_. 1 :: real" "Î»_. _" "Î»x. x", simplified] split: split_indicator cong: conj_cong sum.cong)
    then show "spmf ?lhs i = spmf ?rhs i" using B finA finC A'C C A'
      by(simp add: spmf_bind integral_spmf_of_set sum_Un spmf_of_set field_simps)(simp add: field_simps card_Un_disjoint)
  qed
  finally show ?thesis .
qed(use assms in â€¹auto 4 3 cong: bind_spmf_cong_simp simp add: subsetD bind_spmf_const spmf_of_set_empty disjoint_notin1 intro!: arg_cong[where f=spmf_of_set]â€º)

locale rp_rf =
  rp: random_permutation A +
  rf: random_function "spmf_of_set A"
  for A :: "'a set"
  +
  assumes finite_A: "finite A"
  and nonempty_A: "A â‰  {}"
begin

type_synonym 'a' adversary = "(bool, 'a', 'a') gpv"
  
definition game :: "bool â‡’ 'a adversary â‡’ bool spmf" where
  "game b ğ’œ = run_gpv (if b then rp.random_permutation else rf.random_oracle) ğ’œ Map.empty"
  
abbreviation prp_game :: "'a adversary â‡’ bool spmf" where "prp_game â‰¡ game True"
abbreviation prf_game :: "'a adversary â‡’ bool spmf" where "prf_game â‰¡ game False"
  
definition advantage :: "'a adversary â‡’ real" where
  "advantage ğ’œ = Â¦spmf (prp_game ğ’œ) True - spmf (prf_game ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"
  
lemma advantage_nonneg: "0 â‰¤ advantage ğ’œ" by(simp add: advantage_def)

lemma advantage_le_1: "advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ 1"
  by(auto simp add: advantage_def intro!: abs_leI)(metis diff_0_right diff_left_mono order_trans pmf_le_1 pmf_nonneg) +

context includes â„.lifting begin
lift_definition â„ :: "('a, 'a) â„" is "(Î»x. if x âˆˆ A then A else {})" .
lemma outs_â„_â„ [simp]: "outs_â„ â„ = A" by transfer auto
lemma responses_â„_â„ [simp]: "responses_â„ â„ x = (if x âˆˆ A then A else {})" by transfer simp
lifting_update â„.lifting
lifting_forget â„.lifting
end

lemma rp_rf:
  assumes bound: "interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ q"
    and lossless: "lossless_gpv â„ ğ’œ"
    and WT: "â„ âŠ¢g ğ’œ âˆš"
  shows "advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ q * q / card A"
  including lifting_syntax  
proof -
  let ?run = "Î»b. exec_gpv (if b then rp.random_permutation else rf.random_oracle) ğ’œ Map.empty"
  define rp_bad :: "bool Ã— ('a â‡€ 'a) â‡’ 'a â‡’ ('a Ã— (bool Ã— ('a â‡€ 'a))) spmf"
    where "rp_bad = (Î»(bad, Ïƒ) x. case Ïƒ x of Some y â‡’ return_spmf (y, (bad, Ïƒ))
      | None â‡’ bind_spmf (spmf_of_set A) (Î»y. if y âˆˆ ran Ïƒ then map_spmf (Î»y'. (y', (True, Ïƒ(x â†¦ y')))) (spmf_of_set (A - ran Ïƒ)) else return_spmf (y, (bad, (Ïƒ(x â†¦ y))))))"
  have rp_bad_simps: "rp_bad (bad, Ïƒ) x = (case Ïƒ x of Some y â‡’ return_spmf (y, (bad, Ïƒ))
      | None â‡’ bind_spmf (spmf_of_set A) (Î»y. if y âˆˆ ran Ïƒ then map_spmf (Î»y'. (y', (True, Ïƒ(x â†¦ y')))) (spmf_of_set (A - ran Ïƒ)) else return_spmf (y, (bad, (Ïƒ(x â†¦ y))))))"
    for bad Ïƒ x by(simp add: rp_bad_def)

  let ?S = "rel_prod2 (=)"
  define init :: "bool Ã— ('a â‡€ 'a)" where "init = (False, Map.empty)"
  have rp: "rp.random_permutation = (Î»Ïƒ x. case Ïƒ x of Some y â‡’ return_spmf (y, Ïƒ) 
    | None â‡’ bind_spmf (bind_spmf (spmf_of_set A) (Î»y. if y âˆˆ ran Ïƒ then spmf_of_set (A - ran Ïƒ) else return_spmf y)) (Î»y. return_spmf (y, Ïƒ(x â†¦ y))))"
    by(subst rp_resample)(auto simp add: finite_A rp.random_permutation_def[abs_def])
  have [transfer_rule]: "(?S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) ?S)) rp.random_permutation rp_bad"
    unfolding rp rp_bad_def
    by(auto simp add: rel_fun_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf split: option.split intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
  have [transfer_rule]: "?S Map.empty init" by(simp add: init_def)
  have "spmf (prp_game ğ’œ) True = spmf (run_gpv rp_bad ğ’œ init) True"
    unfolding vimage_def game_def if_True by transfer_prover
  moreover {
    define collision :: "('a â‡€ 'a) â‡’ bool" where "collision m âŸ· Â¬ inj_on m (dom m)" for m
    have [simp]: "Â¬ collision Map.empty" by(simp add: collision_def)
    have [simp]: "âŸ¦ collision m; m x = None âŸ§ âŸ¹ collision (m(x := y))" for m x y
      by(auto simp add: collision_def fun_upd_idem dom_minus fun_upd_image dest: inj_on_fun_updD)
    have collision_map_updI: "âŸ¦ m x = None; y âˆˆ ran m âŸ§ âŸ¹ collision (m(x â†¦ y))" for m x y
      by(auto simp add: collision_def ran_def intro: rev_image_eqI)
    have collision_map_upd_iff: "Â¬ collision m âŸ¹ collision (m(x â†¦ y)) âŸ· y âˆˆ ran m âˆ§ m x â‰  Some y" for m x y
      by(auto simp add: collision_def ran_def fun_upd_idem intro: inj_on_fun_updI rev_image_eqI dest: inj_on_eq_iff)
  
    let ?bad1 = "collision" and ?bad2 = "fst"
      and ?X = "Î»Ïƒ1 (bad, Ïƒ2). Ïƒ1 = Ïƒ2 âˆ§ Â¬ collision Ïƒ1 âˆ§ Â¬ bad"
      and ?I1 = "Î»Ïƒ1. dom Ïƒ1 âŠ† A âˆ§ ran Ïƒ1 âŠ† A"
      and ?I2 = "Î»(bad, Ïƒ2). dom Ïƒ2 âŠ† A âˆ§ ran Ïƒ2 âŠ† A"
    let ?X_bad = "Î»Ïƒ1 s2. ?I1 Ïƒ1 âˆ§ ?I2 s2"
    have [simp]: "â„ âŠ¢c rf.random_oracle s1 âˆš" if "ran s1 âŠ† A" for s1 using that
      by(intro WT_calleeI)(auto simp add: rf.random_oracle_def[abs_def] finite_A nonempty_A ran_def split: option.split_asm)
    have [simp]: "callee_invariant_on rf.random_oracle ?I1 â„"
      by(unfold_locales)(auto simp add: rf.random_oracle_def finite_A split: option.split_asm)
    then interpret rf: callee_invariant_on rf.random_oracle ?I1 â„ .
    have [simp]: "â„ âŠ¢c rp_bad s2 âˆš " if "ran (snd s2) âŠ† A" for s2 using that
      by(intro WT_calleeI)(auto simp add: rp_bad_def finite_A split: prod.split_asm option.split_asm if_split_asm intro: ranI)
    have [simp]: "callee_invariant_on rf.random_oracle (Î»Ïƒ1. ?bad1 Ïƒ1 âˆ§ ?I1 Ïƒ1) â„"
      by(unfold_locales)(clarsimp simp add: rf.random_oracle_def finite_A  split: option.split_asm)+
    have [simp]: "callee_invariant_on rp_bad (Î»s2. ?I2 s2) â„"
      by(unfold_locales)(auto 4 3 simp add: rp_bad_simps finite_A split: option.splits if_split_asm iff del: domIff)
    have [simp]: "callee_invariant_on rp_bad (Î»s2. ?bad2 s2 âˆ§ ?I2 s2) â„"
      by(unfold_locales)(auto 4 3 simp add: rp_bad_simps finite_A split: option.splits if_split_asm iff del: domIff)
    have [simp]: "â„ âŠ¢c rp_bad (bad, Ïƒ2) âˆš" if "ran Ïƒ2 âŠ† A" for bad Ïƒ2 using that
      by(intro WT_calleeI)(auto simp add: rp_bad_def finite_A nonempty_A ran_def split: option.split_asm if_split_asm)
    have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (rp_bad (b, Ïƒ2) x)" if "x âˆˆ A" "dom Ïƒ2 âŠ† A" "ran Ïƒ2 âŠ† A" for b Ïƒ2 x
      using finite_A that unfolding rp_bad_def
      by(clarsimp simp add: nonempty_A dom_subset_ran_iff eq_None_iff_not_dom split: option.split)
    have "rel_spmf (Î»(b1, Ïƒ1) (b2, state2). (?bad1 Ïƒ1 âŸ· ?bad2 state2) âˆ§ (if ?bad2 state2 then ?X_bad Ïƒ1 state2 else b1 = b2 âˆ§ ?X Ïƒ1 state2))
            ((if False then rp.random_permutation else rf.random_oracle) s1 x) (rp_bad s2 x)"
      if "?X s1 s2" "x âˆˆ outs_â„ â„" "?I1 s1" "?I2 s2" for s1 s2 x using that finite_A
      by(auto split!: option.split simp add: rf.random_oracle_def rp_bad_def rel_spmf_return_spmf1 collision_map_updI dom_subset_ran_iff eq_None_iff_not_dom collision_map_upd_iff intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
    with _ _ have "rel_spmf
       (Î»(b1, Ïƒ1) (b2, state2). (?bad1 Ïƒ1 âŸ· ?bad2 state2) âˆ§ (if ?bad2 state2 then ?X_bad Ïƒ1 state2 else b1 = b2 âˆ§ ?X Ïƒ1 state2))
       (?run False) (exec_gpv rp_bad ğ’œ init)"
      by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim_bad_invariant[where â„ = â„ and ?I1.0 = "?I1" and ?I2.0="?I2"])(auto simp add: init_def WT lossless finite_A nonempty_A)
   then have "Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst (?run False)) True - spmf (run_gpv rp_bad ğ’œ init) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ spmf (map_spmf (?bad1 âˆ˜ snd) (?run False)) True"
      unfolding spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def
      by(intro fundamental_lemma[where ?bad2.0="Î»(_, s2). ?bad2 s2"])(auto simp add: split_def elim: rel_spmf_mono)
    also have "ennreal â€¦ â‰¤ ennreal (q / card A) * (enat q)" unfolding if_False using bound _ _ _ _ _ _ _ WT
      by(rule rf.interaction_bounded_by_exec_gpv_bad_count[where count="Î»s. card (dom s)"])
        (auto simp add: rf.random_oracle_def finite_A nonempty_A card_insert_if finite_subset[OF _ finite_A] map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] spmf.map_comp o_def collision_map_upd_iff map_mem_spmf_of_set card_gt_0_iff card_mono field_simps Int_absorb2 intro: card_ran_le_dom[OF finite_subset, OF _ finite_A, THEN order_trans] split: option.splits)
    hence "spmf (map_spmf (?bad1 âˆ˜ snd) (?run False)) True â‰¤ q * q / card A"
      by(simp add: ennreal_of_nat_eq_real_of_nat ennreal_times_divide ennreal_mult''[symmetric])
    finally have "Â¦spmf (run_gpv rp_bad ğ’œ init) True - spmf (run_gpv rf.random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ q * q / card A"
      by simp }
  ultimately show ?thesis by(simp add: advantage_def game_def)
qed

end

Theory PRF_UHF

theory PRF_UHF
imports GPV_Bisim Pseudo_Random_Function
(* Title: PRF_UHF.thy 
  Author: Bhargav Bhatt, ETH Zurich
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹Extending the input length of a PRF using a universal hash functionâ€º

text â€¹ This example is taken from \cite[\S 4.2]{Shoup2004IACR}.â€º

theory PRF_UHF imports
  CryptHOL.GPV_Bisim
  Pseudo_Random_Function
begin

locale "hash" =
  fixes seed_gen :: "'seed spmf"
  and "hash" :: "'seed â‡’ 'domain â‡’ 'range"
begin

definition game_hash :: " 'domain â‡’ 'domain â‡’ bool spmf"
where 
 "game_hash w w' = do {
    seed â† seed_gen;
    return_spmf (hash seed w = hash seed w' âˆ§ w â‰  w')
  }"

definition game_hash_set :: "'domain set â‡’ bool spmf"
where 
  "game_hash_set W = do {
     seed  â† seed_gen;
     return_spmf (Â¬ inj_on (hash seed) W)
   }"

definition Îµ_uh :: "real"
where "Îµ_uh  = (SUP w w'. spmf (game_hash w w') True)"

lemma Îµ_uh_nonneg : "Îµ_uh â‰¥ 0"
by(auto 4 3 intro!: cSUP_upper2 bdd_aboveI2[where M=1] cSUP_least pmf_le_1 pmf_nonneg simp add: Îµ_uh_def)

lemma hash_ineq_card:
  assumes "finite W"
  shows "spmf (game_hash_set W) True â‰¤ Îµ_uh * card W * card W" 
proof -
  let ?M = "measure (measure_spmf seed_gen)"
  have bound: "?M {x. hash x w = hash x w' âˆ§ w â‰  w'} â‰¤ Îµ_uh" for w w'
  proof -
    have "?M {x. hash x w = hash x w' âˆ§ w â‰  w'} = spmf (game_hash w w') True"
      by(simp add: game_hash_def spmf_conv_measure_spmf map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] measure_map_spmf vimage_def)
    also have "â€¦ â‰¤ Îµ_uh" unfolding Îµ_uh_def
      by(auto intro!: cSUP_upper2 bdd_aboveI[where M=1] cSUP_least simp add: pmf_le_1)
    finally show ?thesis .
  qed

  have "spmf (game_hash_set W) True = ?M {x. âˆƒxaâˆˆW. âˆƒyâˆˆW. hash x xa = hash x y âˆ§ xa â‰  y}"
    by(auto simp add: game_hash_set_def inj_on_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def)
  also have "{x. âˆƒxaâˆˆW. âˆƒyâˆˆW. hash x xa = hash x y âˆ§ xa â‰  y} = (â‹ƒ(w, w') âˆˆ WÃ— W. {x. hash x w = hash x w' âˆ§ w â‰  w'})"
    by(auto)
  also have "?M â€¦ â‰¤ (âˆ‘(w, w')âˆˆW Ã— W. ?M {x. hash x w = hash x w' âˆ§ w â‰  w'})"
    by(auto intro!: measure_spmf.finite_measure_subadditive_finite simp add: split_def assms)
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ (âˆ‘(w, w')âˆˆW Ã— W. Îµ_uh)" by(rule sum_mono)(clarsimp simp add: bound)
  also have "â€¦ =  Îµ_uh * card(W) * card(W)" by(simp add: card_cartesian_product)
  finally show ?thesis .
qed

end 

locale prf_hash =
  fixes f :: "'key â‡’ 'Î± â‡’ 'Î³"
  and h :: "'seed â‡’ 'Î² â‡’ 'Î±"
  and key_gen :: "'key spmf"
  and seed_gen :: "'seed spmf"
  and range_f :: "'Î³ set"
  assumes lossless_seed_gen: "lossless_spmf seed_gen"
  and range_f_finite: "finite range_f"
  and range_f_nonempty: "range_f â‰  {}"
begin

definition rand :: "'Î³ spmf"
where "rand = spmf_of_set range_f"

lemma lossless_rand [simp]: "lossless_spmf rand"
by(simp add: rand_def range_f_finite range_f_nonempty)

definition key_seed_gen :: "('key * 'seed) spmf"
where
  "key_seed_gen = do {
     k â† key_gen;
     s :: 'seed â† seed_gen;
     return_spmf (k, s)
   }"

interpretation "prf": "prf" key_gen f rand .
interpretation hash: hash "seed_gen" "h".

fun f' :: "'key Ã— 'seed â‡’ 'Î² â‡’ 'Î³"
where "f' (key, seed) x = f key (h seed x)"

interpretation "prf'": "prf" key_seed_gen f' rand .

definition reduction_oracle :: "'seed â‡’ unit â‡’ 'Î² â‡’ ('Î³ Ã— unit, 'Î±, 'Î³) gpv"
where "reduction_oracle seed x b = Pause (h seed b) (Î»x. Done (x, ()))" 

definition prf'_reduction :: " ('Î², 'Î³) prf'.adversary â‡’ ('Î±, 'Î³) prf.adversary"
where
  "prf'_reduction ğ’œ = do {
      seed  â† lift_spmf seed_gen;
      (b, Ïƒ) â† inline (reduction_oracle seed) ğ’œ ();
      Done b
  }"

theorem prf_prf'_advantage: 
  assumes "prf'.lossless ğ’œ"
  and bounded: "prf'.ibounded_by ğ’œ q" 
  shows "prf'.advantage ğ’œ  â‰¤ prf.advantage (prf'_reduction ğ’œ) + hash.Îµ_uh * q * q"
  including lifting_syntax
proof -
  let ?ğ’œ = "prf'_reduction ğ’œ"

  { define cr where "cr = (Î»_ :: unit Ã— unit. Î»_ :: unit. True)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "cr ((), ()) ()" by(simp add: cr_def)
    have "prf.game_0 ?ğ’œ = prf'.game_0 ğ’œ"
      unfolding prf'.game_0_def prf.game_0_def prf'_reduction_def unfolding key_seed_gen_def
      by(simp add: exec_gpv_bind split_def exec_gpv_inline reduction_oracle_def bind_map_spmf prf.prf_oracle_def prf'.prf_oracle_def[abs_def]) 
        (transfer_prover) }
  note hop1 = this[symmetric]

  define semi_forgetful_RO where "semi_forgetful_RO = (Î»seed :: 'seed. Î»(Ïƒ :: 'Î± â‡€ 'Î² Ã— 'Î³, b :: bool). Î»x. 
    case Ïƒ (h seed x) of Some (a, y) â‡’ return_spmf (y, (Ïƒ, a â‰  x âˆ¨ b))
     | None â‡’ bind_spmf rand (Î»y. return_spmf (y, (Ïƒ(h seed x â†¦ (x, y)), b))))"

  define game_semi_forgetful where "game_semi_forgetful = do {
     seed :: 'seed â† seed_gen;
     (b, rep) â† exec_gpv (semi_forgetful_RO seed) ğ’œ (Map.empty, False);
     return_spmf (b, rep) 
   }"

  have bad_semi_forgetful [simp]: "callee_invariant (semi_forgetful_RO seed) snd" for seed
    by(unfold_locales)(auto simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def split: option.split_asm)
  have lossless_semi_forgetful [simp]: "lossless_spmf (semi_forgetful_RO seed s1 x)" for seed s1 x
    by(simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def split_def split: option.split)

  { define cr
      where "cr = (Î»(_ :: unit, Ïƒ) (Ïƒ' :: 'Î± â‡’ ('Î² Ã— 'Î³) option, _ :: bool). Ïƒ = map_option snd âˆ˜ Ïƒ')"
    define initial where "initial = (Map.empty :: 'Î± â‡’ ('Î² Ã— 'Î³) option, False)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "cr ((), Map.empty) initial" by(simp add: cr_def initial_def fun_eq_iff)
    have [transfer_rule]:  "((=) ===> cr ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) cr))
        (Î»y p ya. do {y â† prf.random_oracle (snd p) (h y ya); return_spmf (fst y, (), snd y) })
        semi_forgetful_RO"
      by(auto simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def cr_def prf.random_oracle_def rel_fun_def fun_eq_iff split: option.split intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
    have "prf.game_1 ?ğ’œ = map_spmf fst game_semi_forgetful"
      unfolding prf.game_1_def prf'_reduction_def game_semi_forgetful_def
      by(simp add: exec_gpv_bind exec_gpv_inline split_def bind_map_spmf map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf reduction_oracle_def initial_def[symmetric])
        (transfer_prover) }
  note hop2 = this

  define game_semi_forgetful_bad where "game_semi_forgetful_bad = do {
       seed :: 'seed â† seed_gen;
       x â† exec_gpv (semi_forgetful_RO seed) ğ’œ (Map.empty, False);
       return_spmf (snd x) 
       }"
  have game_semi_forgetful_bad : "map_spmf snd game_semi_forgetful = game_semi_forgetful_bad"
    unfolding game_semi_forgetful_bad_def game_semi_forgetful_def
    by(simp add: map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def)

  have bad_random_oracle_A [simp]: "callee_invariant prf.random_oracle (Î»Ïƒ. Â¬ inj_on (h seed) (dom Ïƒ))" for seed
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: prf.random_oracle_def split: option.split_asm)

  define invar
    where "invar = (Î»seed (Ïƒ1, b) (Ïƒ2 :: 'Î² â‡’ 'Î³ option). Â¬ b âˆ§ dom Ïƒ1 = h seed ` dom Ïƒ2 âˆ§ 
      (âˆ€x âˆˆ dom Ïƒ2. Ïƒ1 (h seed x) = map_option (Pair x) (Ïƒ2 x)))"

  have rel_spmf_oracle_adv: 
    "rel_spmf (Î»(x, s1) (y, s2). snd s1 â‰  inj_on (h seed) (dom s2) âˆ§ (inj_on (h seed) (dom s2) âŸ¶ x = y âˆ§ invar seed s1 s2))
      (exec_gpv (semi_forgetful_RO seed) ğ’œ (Map.empty, False))
      (exec_gpv prf.random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty)"
    if seed: "seed âˆˆ set_spmf seed_gen" for seed
  proof -
    have invar_initial [simp]: "invar seed (Map.empty, False) Map.empty" by(simp add: invar_def)
    have invarD_inj: "inj_on (h seed) (dom s2)" if "invar seed bs1 s2" for bs1 s2
      using that by(auto intro!: inj_onI simp add: invar_def)(metis domI domIff option.map_sel prod.inject)

    let ?R = "Î»(a, s1) (b, s2 :: 'Î² â‡’ 'Î³ option).
        snd s1 = (Â¬ inj_on (h seed) (dom s2)) âˆ§
        (Â¬ Â¬ inj_on (h seed) (dom s2) âŸ¶ a = b âˆ§ invar seed s1 s2)"

    have step: "rel_spmf ?R (semi_forgetful_RO seed Ïƒ1b x) (prf.random_oracle s2 x)"
      if X: "invar seed Ïƒ1b s2" for s2 Ïƒ1b x
    proof -
      obtain Ïƒ1 b where [simp]: "Ïƒ1b = (Ïƒ1, b)" by(cases Ïƒ1b)
      from X have not_b: "Â¬ b"
        and dom: "dom Ïƒ1 = h seed ` dom s2"
        and eq: "âˆ€xâˆˆdom s2. Ïƒ1 (h seed x) = map_option (Pair x) (s2 x)" 
        by(simp_all add: invar_def)
      from X have inj: "inj_on (h seed) (dom s2)" by(rule invarD_inj)
  
      have not_in_image: "h seed x âˆ‰ h seed ` (dom s2 - {x})" if "Ïƒ1 (h seed x) = None"
      proof (rule notI)
        assume "h seed x âˆˆ h seed ` (dom s2 - {x})"
        then obtain y where "y âˆˆ dom s2" and hx_hy: "h seed x = h seed y" by (auto)
        then have "Ïƒ1 (h seed y) = None" using that by (auto)
        then have "h seed y âˆ‰ h seed ` dom s2" using dom by (auto)
        then have "y âˆ‰ dom s2" by (auto)
        then show False using â€¹y âˆˆ dom s2â€º by(auto)
      qed
  
      show ?thesis
      proof(cases "Ïƒ1 (h seed x)")
        case Ïƒ1: None
        hence s2: "s2 x = None" using dom by(auto)
        have "insert (h seed x) (dom Ïƒ1) = insert (h seed x) (h seed ` dom s2)" by(simp add: dom)
        then have invar_update: "invar seed (Ïƒ1(h seed x â†¦ (x, bs)), False) (s2(x â†¦ bs))" for bs
          using inj not_b not_in_image Ïƒ1 dom
          by(auto simp add: invar_def domIff eq) (metis domI domIff imageI)
        with Ïƒ1 s2 show ?thesis using inj not_b not_in_image
          by(auto simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def prf.random_oracle_def intro: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
      next
        case Ïƒ1: (Some "by")
        show ?thesis
        proof(cases "s2 x")
          case s2: (Some z)
          with eq Ïƒ1 have "by = (x, z)" by(auto simp add: domIff)
          thus ?thesis using Ïƒ1 inj not_b s2 X
            by(simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def prf.random_oracle_def split_beta)
        next
          case s2: None
          from Ïƒ1 dom obtain y where y: "y âˆˆ dom s2" and *: "h seed x = h seed y" 
            by(metis domIff imageE option.distinct(1))
          from y obtain z where z: "s2 y = Some z" by auto
          from eq z Ïƒ1 have "by": "by = (y, z)" by(auto simp add: * domIff)
          from y s2 have xny: "x â‰  y" by auto
          with y * have "h seed x âˆˆ h seed ` (dom s2 - {x})" by auto
          then show ?thesis using Ïƒ1 s2 not_b "by" xny inj
            by(simp add: semi_forgetful_RO_def prf.random_oracle_def split_beta)(rule rel_spmf_bindI2; simp)
        qed
      qed
    qed
    from invar_initial _ step show ?thesis
      by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim_bad_full[where ?bad1.0 = "snd" and ?bad2.0 = "Î»Ïƒ. Â¬ inj_on (h seed) (dom Ïƒ)"])
        (simp_all add: assms)
  qed

  define game_A where "game_A = do {
      seed :: 'seed â† seed_gen;
      (b, Ïƒ) â† exec_gpv prf.random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty;
      return_spmf (b, Â¬ inj_on (h seed) (dom Ïƒ))
    }"

  let ?bad1 = "Î»x. snd (snd x)" and ?bad2 = "snd"
  have hop3: "rel_spmf (Î»x xa. (?bad1 x âŸ· ?bad2 xa) âˆ§ (Â¬ ?bad2 xa âŸ¶ fst x âŸ· fst xa)) game_semi_forgetful game_A"
    unfolding game_semi_forgetful_def game_A_def 
    by(clarsimp simp add: restrict_bind_spmf split_def map_spmf_bind_spmf restrict_return_spmf o_def intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI simp del: bind_return_spmf)
      (rule rel_spmf_bindI[OF rel_spmf_oracle_adv]; auto)
  have bad1_bad2: "spmf (map_spmf (snd âˆ˜ snd) game_semi_forgetful) True = spmf (map_spmf snd game_A) True"
    using fundamental_lemma_bad[OF hop3] by(simp add: measure_map_spmf spmf_conv_measure_spmf vimage_def)
  have bound_bad1_event: "Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game_semi_forgetful) True - spmf (map_spmf fst game_A) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ spmf (map_spmf (snd âˆ˜ snd) game_semi_forgetful) True"
    using fundamental_lemma[OF hop3] by(simp add: measure_map_spmf spmf_conv_measure_spmf vimage_def)
  
  then have bound_bad2_event : "Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game_semi_forgetful) True - spmf (map_spmf fst game_A) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ spmf (map_spmf snd game_A) True"
    using bad1_bad2 by (simp)
  
  define game_B where "game_B = do {
      (b, Ïƒ) â† exec_gpv prf.random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty;
      hash.game_hash_set (dom Ïƒ)
    }"
  
  have game_A_game_B: "map_spmf snd game_A = game_B"
    unfolding game_B_def game_A_def hash.game_hash_set_def including monad_normalisation
    by(simp add: map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def)
  
  have game_B_bound : "spmf game_B True â‰¤ hash.Îµ_uh * q * q" unfolding game_B_def
  proof(rule spmf_bind_leI, clarify)
    fix b Ïƒ
    assume *: "(b, Ïƒ) âˆˆ set_spmf (exec_gpv prf.random_oracle ğ’œ Map.empty)"
    have "finite (dom Ïƒ)" by(rule prf.finite.exec_gpv_invariant[OF *]) simp_all
    then have "spmf (hash.game_hash_set (dom Ïƒ)) True â‰¤ hash.Îµ_uh * (card (dom Ïƒ) * card (dom Ïƒ))"
      using hash.hash_ineq_card[of "dom Ïƒ"] by simp
    also have p1: "card (dom Ïƒ) â‰¤ q + card (dom (Map.empty :: 'Î² â‡’ 'Î³ option))" 
      by(rule prf.card_dom_random_oracle[OF bounded *]) simp
    then have "card (dom Ïƒ) * card (dom Ïƒ) â‰¤ q * q" using mult_le_mono by auto
    finally show "spmf (hash.game_hash_set (dom Ïƒ)) True â‰¤ hash.Îµ_uh * q * q"
      by(simp add: hash.Îµ_uh_nonneg mult_left_mono)
  qed(simp add: hash.Îµ_uh_nonneg)
  
  have hop4: "prf'.game_1 ğ’œ = map_spmf fst game_A"
    by(simp add: game_A_def prf'.game_1_def map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def bind_spmf_const lossless_seed_gen lossless_weight_spmfD)
  
  have "prf'.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ Â¦spmf (prf.game_0 ?ğ’œ) True - spmf (prf'.game_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"
    using hop1 by(simp add: prf'.advantage_def)
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ prf.advantage ?ğ’œ + Â¦spmf (prf.game_1 ?ğ’œ) True - spmf (prf'.game_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"
    by(simp add: prf.advantage_def)
  also have "Â¦spmf (prf.game_1 ?ğ’œ) True - spmf (prf'.game_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤
    Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game_semi_forgetful) True - spmf (prf'.game_1 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦"
    using hop2 by simp
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ hash.Îµ_uh * q * q"
    using game_A_game_B game_B_bound bound_bad2_event hop4 by(simp)
  finally show ?thesis by(simp add: add_left_mono)
qed

end

end

Theory PRF_IND_CPA

theory PRF_IND_CPA
imports GPV_Bisim List_Bits Pseudo_Random_Function IND_CPA
(* Title: PRF_IND_CPA.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹IND-CPA from PRFâ€º

theory PRF_IND_CPA imports
  CryptHOL.GPV_Bisim
  CryptHOL.List_Bits
  Pseudo_Random_Function
  IND_CPA
begin

text â€¹
  Formalises the construction from \cite{PetcherMorrisett2015POST}.
â€º

declare [[simproc del: let_simp]]

type_synonym key = "bool list"
type_synonym plain = "bool list"
type_synonym cipher = "bool list * bool list"

locale otp =
  fixes f :: "key â‡’ bool list â‡’ bool list"
  and len :: nat
  assumes length_f: "â‹€xs ys. âŸ¦ length xs = len; length ys = len âŸ§ âŸ¹ length (f xs ys) = len"
begin

definition key_gen :: "bool list spmf"
where "key_gen = spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len)"

definition valid_plain :: "plain â‡’ bool"
where "valid_plain plain âŸ· length plain = len"

definition encrypt :: "key â‡’ plain â‡’ cipher spmf"
where
  "encrypt key plain = do {
     r â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len);
     return_spmf (r, xor_list plain (f key r))
   }"

fun decrypt :: "key â‡’ cipher â‡’ plain option"
where "decrypt key (r, c) = Some (xor_list (f key r) c)"

lemma encrypt_decrypt_correct:
  "âŸ¦ length key = len; length plain = len âŸ§
  âŸ¹ encrypt key plain â¤œ (Î»cipher. return_spmf (decrypt key cipher)) = return_spmf (Some plain)"
by(simp add: encrypt_def zip_map2 o_def split_def bind_eq_return_spmf length_f in_nlists_UNIV xor_list_left_commute)

interpretation ind_cpa: ind_cpa key_gen encrypt decrypt valid_plain .
interpretation "prf": "prf" key_gen f "spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len)" .

definition prf_encrypt_oracle :: "unit â‡’ plain â‡’ (cipher Ã— unit, plain, plain) gpv"
where
  "prf_encrypt_oracle x plain = do {
     r â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len));
     Pause r (Î»pad. Done ((r, xor_list plain pad), ()))
  }"

lemma interaction_bounded_by_prf_encrypt_oracle [interaction_bound]:
  "interaction_any_bounded_by (prf_encrypt_oracle Ïƒ plain) 1"
unfolding prf_encrypt_oracle_def by simp

lemma lossless_prf_encyrpt_oracle [simp]: "lossless_gpv â„_top (prf_encrypt_oracle s x)"
by(simp add: prf_encrypt_oracle_def)

definition prf_adversary :: "(plain, cipher, 'state) ind_cpa.adversary â‡’ (plain, plain) prf.adversary"
where
  "prf_adversary ğ’œ = do {
     let (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2) = ğ’œ;
     (((p1, p2), Ïƒ), n) â† inline prf_encrypt_oracle ğ’œ1 ();
     if valid_plain p1 âˆ§ valid_plain p2 then do { 
       b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
       let pb = (if b then p1 else p2);
       r â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len));
       pad â† Pause r Done;
       let c = (r, xor_list pb pad);
       (b', _) â† inline prf_encrypt_oracle (ğ’œ2 c Ïƒ) n;
       Done (b' = b)
     } else lift_spmf coin_spmf
  }"

theorem prf_encrypt_advantage:
  assumes "ind_cpa.ibounded_by ğ’œ q"
  and "lossless_gpv â„_full (fst ğ’œ)"
  and "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_gpv â„_full (snd ğ’œ cipher Ïƒ)"
  shows "ind_cpa.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ prf.advantage (prf_adversary ğ’œ) + q / 2 ^ len"
proof -
  note [split del] = if_split
    and [cong del] = if_weak_cong
    and [simp] =
      bind_spmf_const map_spmf_bind_spmf bind_map_spmf 
      exec_gpv_bind exec_gpv_inline
      rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_reflI
  obtain ğ’œ1 ğ’œ2 where ğ’œ: "ğ’œ = (ğ’œ1, ğ’œ2)" by(cases "ğ’œ")
  from â€¹ind_cpa.ibounded_by _ _â€º
  obtain q1 q2 :: nat
    where q1: "interaction_any_bounded_by ğ’œ1 q1"
    and q2: "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. interaction_any_bounded_by (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) q2"
    and "q1 + q2 â‰¤ q"
    unfolding ğ’œ by(rule ind_cpa.ibounded_byE)(auto simp add: iadd_le_enat_iff)
  from ğ’œ assms have lossless1: "lossless_gpv â„_full ğ’œ1"
    and lossless2: "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_gpv â„_full (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ)" by simp_all
  have weight1: "â‹€oracle s. (â‹€s x. lossless_spmf (oracle s x)) 
    âŸ¹ weight_spmf (exec_gpv oracle ğ’œ1 s) = 1"
    by(rule lossless_weight_spmfD)(rule lossless_exec_gpv[OF lossless1], simp_all)
  have weight2: "â‹€oracle s cipher Ïƒ. (â‹€s x. lossless_spmf (oracle s x)) 
    âŸ¹ weight_spmf (exec_gpv oracle (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s) = 1"
    by(rule lossless_weight_spmfD)(rule lossless_exec_gpv[OF lossless2], simp_all)

  let ?oracle1 = "Î»key (s', s) y. map_spmf (Î»((x, s'), s). (x, (), ())) (exec_gpv (prf.prf_oracle key) (prf_encrypt_oracle () y) ())"
  have bisim1: "â‹€key. rel_spmf (Î»(x, _) (y, _). x = y)
          (exec_gpv (ind_cpa.encrypt_oracle key) ğ’œ1 ())
          (exec_gpv (?oracle1 key) ğ’œ1 ((), ()))"
    using TrueI
    by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim)(auto simp add: encrypt_def prf_encrypt_oracle_def ind_cpa.encrypt_oracle_def prf.prf_oracle_def o_def)
  have bisim2: "â‹€key cipher Ïƒ. rel_spmf (Î»(x, _) (y, _). x = y)
             (exec_gpv (ind_cpa.encrypt_oracle key) (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) ())
             (exec_gpv (?oracle1 key) (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) ((), ()))"
    using TrueI
    by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim)(auto simp add: encrypt_def prf_encrypt_oracle_def ind_cpa.encrypt_oracle_def prf.prf_oracle_def o_def)
   
  have ind_cpa_0: "rel_spmf (=) (ind_cpa.ind_cpa ğ’œ) (prf.game_0 (prf_adversary ğ’œ))"
    unfolding IND_CPA.ind_cpa.ind_cpa_def ğ’œ key_gen_def Let_def prf_adversary_def Pseudo_Random_Function.prf.game_0_def
    apply(simp)
    apply(rewrite in "bind_spmf _ âŒ‘" bind_commute_spmf)
    apply(rule rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
    apply(rule rel_spmf_bindI[OF bisim1])
    apply(clarsimp simp add: if_distribs bind_coin_spmf_eq_const')
    apply(auto intro: rel_spmf_bindI[OF bisim2] intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI simp add: encrypt_def prf.prf_oracle_def cong del: if_cong)
    done

  define rf_encrypt where "rf_encrypt = (Î»s plain. bind_spmf (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len)) (Î»r :: bool list. 
    bind_spmf (prf.random_oracle s r) (Î»(pad, s'). 
    return_spmf ((r, xor_list plain pad), s')))
  )"
  interpret rf_finite: callee_invariant_on rf_encrypt "Î»s. finite (dom s)" â„_full
    by unfold_locales(auto simp add: rf_encrypt_def dest: prf.finite.callee_invariant)
  have lossless_rf_encrypt [simp]: "â‹€s plain. lossless_spmf (rf_encrypt s plain)"
    by(auto simp add: rf_encrypt_def)

  define game2 where "game2 = do {
    (((p0, p1), Ïƒ), s1) â† exec_gpv rf_encrypt ğ’œ1 Map.empty;
    if valid_plain p0 âˆ§ valid_plain p1 then do {
      b â† coin_spmf;
      let pb = (if b then p0 else p1);
      (cipher, s2) â† rf_encrypt s1 pb;
      (b', s3) â† exec_gpv rf_encrypt (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s2;
      return_spmf (b' = b)
    } else coin_spmf
  }"

  let ?oracle2 = "Î»(s', s) y. map_spmf (Î»((x, s'), s). (x, (), s)) (exec_gpv prf.random_oracle (prf_encrypt_oracle () y) s)"
  let ?I = "Î»(x, _, s) (y, s'). x = y âˆ§ s = s'"
  have bisim1: "rel_spmf ?I (exec_gpv ?oracle2 ğ’œ1 ((), Map.empty)) (exec_gpv rf_encrypt ğ’œ1 Map.empty)"
     by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim[where X="Î»(_, s) s'. s = s'"])
       (auto simp add: rf_encrypt_def prf_encrypt_oracle_def intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
  have bisim2: "â‹€cipher Ïƒ s. rel_spmf ?I (exec_gpv ?oracle2 (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) ((), s)) (exec_gpv rf_encrypt (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s)"
    by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim[where X="Î»(_, s) s'. s = s'"])
      (auto simp add: prf_encrypt_oracle_def rf_encrypt_def intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)

    by(rewrite in "if _ then âŒ‘ else _" rf_encrypt_def)
      (auto simp add: Let_def ğ’œ if_distribs intro!: rel_spmf_bindI[OF bisim2] rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_bindI[OF bisim1])

  define game2_a where "game2_a = do {

  define game2_b where "game2_b = do {

  have "game2 = do {

  define rf_encrypt_bad
    where "rf_encrypt_bad = (Î»secret (s :: (plain, plain) prf.dict, bad) plain. bind_spmf

  { fix cipher Ïƒ and x :: plain and s r

  ultimately have game2c_2d: "Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game2_c) True - spmf (map_spmf fst game2_d) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ spmf (map_spmf snd game2_c) True"

  { fix cipher Ïƒ and challenge :: plain and s
    have "card (nlists UNIV len âˆ© (Î»x. x = challenge) -` {True}) â‰¤ card {challenge}"
      by(rule card_mono) auto
    then have "spmf (map_spmf (snd âˆ˜ snd) (exec_gpv (rf_encrypt_bad challenge) (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, False))) True â‰¤ (1 / 2 ^ len) * q2"

    hence "(âˆ«â‡§+ x. ennreal (indicator {True} x) âˆ‚measure_spmf (map_spmf (snd âˆ˜ snd) (exec_gpv (rf_encrypt_bad challenge) (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, False)))) â‰¤ (1 / 2 ^ len) * q2"
      by(simp only: ennreal_indicator nn_integral_indicator sets_measure_spmf sets_count_space Pow_UNIV UNIV_I emeasure_spmf_single) simp }
  then have "spmf (map_spmf snd game2_d) True â‰¤
        âˆ«â‡§+ (r :: plain). âˆ«â‡§+ (((p0, p1), Ïƒ), s). (if valid_plain p0 âˆ§ valid_plain p1 then
             âˆ«â‡§+ b . âˆ«â‡§+ (pad :: plain). q2 / 2 ^ len âˆ‚measure_spmf (spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV len)) âˆ‚measure_spmf coin_spmf
              else 0)

  finally have game2_d_bad: "spmf (map_spmf snd game2_d) True â‰¤ q2 / 2 ^ len" by simp

  define game3 where "game3 = do {
      (((p0, p1), Ïƒ), s1) â† exec_gpv rf_encrypt ğ’œ1 Map.empty;
      if valid_plain p0 âˆ§ valid_plain p1 then do {
        b â† coin_spmf;

      } else coin_spmf

  have bisim2d_3: "â‹€cipher Ïƒ s r. rel_spmf (Î»(x, _) (y, _). x = y)
             (exec_gpv (rf_encrypt_bad r) (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) (s, False))
             (exec_gpv rf_encrypt (ğ’œ2 cipher Ïƒ) s)"
    by(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim[where X="Î»(s1, _) s2. s1 = s2"])(auto simp add: rf_encrypt_bad_def rf_encrypt_def intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI)
  have game2d_3: "rel_spmf (=) (map_spmf fst game2_d) game3"
    unfolding game2_d_def game3_def Let_def including monad_normalisation
    by(clarsimp simp add: o_def split_def if_distribs cong: if_cong intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_bindI[OF bisim2d_3])

  have "Â¦spmf game2 True - 1 / 2Â¦ â‰¤
    Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game2_a) True - spmf (map_spmf fst game2_b) TrueÂ¦ + Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game2_b) True - 1 / 2Â¦"

    Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game2_c) True - spmf (map_spmf fst game2_d) TrueÂ¦ + Â¦spmf (map_spmf fst game2_d) True - 1 / 2Â¦"

  finally (add_left_mono_trans) 
  have game2: "Â¦spmf game2 True - 1 / 2Â¦ â‰¤ q1 / 2 ^ len + q2 / 2 ^ len +  Â¦spmf game3 True - 1 / 2Â¦"
    using game2d_3 by(simp add: field_simps spmf_rel_eq)

  have "game3 = do {
      (((p0, p1), Ïƒ), s1) â† exec_gpv rf_encrypt ğ’œ1 Map.empty;
      if valid_plain p0 âˆ§ valid_plain p1 then do {

  also have "â€¦ = do {

  also have "â€¦ = do {

  have "ind_cpa.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ prf.advantage (prf_adversary ğ’œ) + Â¦spmf (prf.game_1 (prf_adversary ğ’œ)) True - 1 / 2Â¦"

    using game1_2 game2 game3 by(simp add: spmf_of_set)
  also have "â€¦ = (q1 + q2) / 2 ^ len" by(simp add: field_simps)
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ q / 2 ^ len" using â€¹q1 + q2 â‰¤ qâ€º by(simp add: divide_right_mono)
  finally show ?thesis by(simp add: field_simps)
qed

lemma interaction_bounded_prf_adversary: 
  fixes q :: nat
  assumes "ind_cpa.ibounded_by ğ’œ q"
  shows "prf.ibounded_by (prf_adversary ğ’œ) (1 + q)"
proof -
  fix Î·
  from assms have "ind_cpa.ibounded_by ğ’œ q" by blast
  then obtain q1 q2 where q: "q1 + q2 â‰¤ q"
    and [interaction_bound]: "interaction_any_bounded_by (fst ğ’œ) q1"
       "â‹€x Ïƒ. interaction_any_bounded_by (snd ğ’œ x Ïƒ) q2"
    unfolding ind_cpa.ibounded_by_def by(auto simp add: split_beta iadd_le_enat_iff)
  show "prf.ibounded_by (prf_adversary ğ’œ) (1 + q)" using q
    apply (simp only: prf_adversary_def Let_def split_def)
    apply -
    apply interaction_bound
      apply (auto simp add: iadd_SUP_le_iff SUP_le_iff add.assoc [symmetric] one_enat_def cong del: image_cong_simp cong add: SUP_cong_simp)
    done 
qed

lemma lossless_prf_adversary: "ind_cpa.lossless ğ’œ âŸ¹ prf.lossless (prf_adversary ğ’œ)"
by(fastforce simp add: prf_adversary_def Let_def split_def ind_cpa.lossless_def intro: lossless_inline)

end

locale otp_Î· =
  fixes f :: "security â‡’ key â‡’ bool list â‡’ bool list"
  and len :: "security â‡’ nat"
  assumes length_f: "â‹€Î· xs ys. âŸ¦ length xs = len Î·; length ys = len Î· âŸ§ âŸ¹ length (f Î· xs ys) = len Î·"
  and negligible_len [negligible_intros]: "negligible (Î»Î·. 1 / 2 ^ (len Î·))"
begin

interpretation otp "f Î·" "len Î·" for Î· by(unfold_locales)(rule length_f)
interpretation ind_cpa: ind_cpa "key_gen Î·" "encrypt Î·" "decrypt Î·" "valid_plain Î·" for Î· .
interpretation "prf": "prf" "key_gen Î·" "f Î·" "spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV (len Î·))" for Î· .

lemma prf_encrypt_secure_for:
  assumes [negligible_intros]: "negligible (Î»Î·. prf.advantage Î· (prf_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)))"
  and q: "â‹€Î·. ind_cpa.ibounded_by (ğ’œ Î·) (q Î·)" and [negligible_intros]: "polynomial q"
  and lossless: "â‹€Î·. ind_cpa.lossless (ğ’œ Î·)"
  shows "negligible (Î»Î·. ind_cpa.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·))"
proof(rule negligible_mono)
  show "negligible (Î»Î·. prf.advantage Î· (prf_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) + q Î· / 2 ^ len Î·)"
    by(intro negligible_intros)
  { fix Î·
    from â€¹ind_cpa.ibounded_by _ _â€º have "ind_cpa.ibounded_by (ğ’œ Î·) (q Î·)" by blast
    moreover from lossless have "ind_cpa.lossless (ğ’œ Î·)" by blast
    hence "lossless_gpv â„_full (fst (ğ’œ Î·))" "â‹€cipher Ïƒ. lossless_gpv â„_full (snd (ğ’œ Î·) cipher Ïƒ)"
      by(auto simp add: ind_cpa.lossless_def)
    ultimately have "ind_cpa.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·) â‰¤ prf.advantage Î· (prf_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) + q Î· / 2 ^ len Î·"
      by(rule prf_encrypt_advantage) }
  hence "eventually (Î»Î·. Â¦ind_cpa.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·)Â¦ â‰¤ 1 * Â¦prf.advantage Î· (prf_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) + q Î· / 2 ^ len Î·Â¦) at_top"
    by(simp add: always_eventually ind_cpa.advantage_nonneg prf.advantage_nonneg)
  then show "(Î»Î·. ind_cpa.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) âˆˆ O(Î»Î·. prf.advantage Î· (prf_adversary Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) + q Î· / 2 ^ len Î·)"
    by(intro bigoI[where c=1]) simp
qed

end

end

Theory PRF_UPF_IND_CCA

theory PRF_UPF_IND_CCA
imports Pseudo_Random_Function List_Bits Unpredictable_Function IND_CCA2_sym Negligible
(* Title: PRF_UPF_IND_CCA.thy
  Author: Andreas Lochbihler, ETH Zurich 
  Author: S. Reza Sefidgar, ETH Zurich *)

subsection â€¹IND-CCA from a PRF and an unpredictable functionâ€º

theory PRF_UPF_IND_CCA
imports
  Pseudo_Random_Function
  CryptHOL.List_Bits
  Unpredictable_Function
  IND_CCA2_sym
  CryptHOL.Negligible
begin

text â€¹Formalisation of Shoup's construction of an IND-CCA secure cipher from a PRF and an unpredictable function \cite[\S 7]{Shoup2004IACR}.â€º

type_synonym bitstring = "bool list"

locale simple_cipher = 
  PRF: "prf" prf_key_gen prf_fun "spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV prf_clen)" +
  UPF: upf upf_key_gen upf_fun
  for prf_key_gen :: "'prf_key spmf"
  and prf_fun :: "'prf_key â‡’ bitstring â‡’ bitstring"
  and prf_domain :: "bitstring set"
  and prf_range :: "bitstring set"
  and prf_dlen :: nat
  and prf_clen :: nat
  and upf_key_gen :: "'upf_key spmf"
  and upf_fun :: "'upf_key â‡’ bitstring â‡’ 'hash"
  +
  assumes prf_domain_finite: "finite prf_domain"
  assumes prf_domain_nonempty: "prf_domain â‰  {}"
  assumes prf_domain_length:  "x âˆˆ prf_domain âŸ¹ length x = prf_dlen"
  assumes prf_codomain_length: 
    "âŸ¦ key_prf âˆˆ set_spmf prf_key_gen; m âˆˆ prf_domain âŸ§ âŸ¹ length (prf_fun key_prf m) = prf_clen"
  assumes prf_key_gen_lossless: "lossless_spmf prf_key_gen"
  assumes upf_key_gen_lossless: "lossless_spmf upf_key_gen"
begin

type_synonym 'hash' cipher_text = "bitstring Ã— bitstring Ã— 'hash'"

definition key_gen :: "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) spmf" where
 "key_gen = do {
   k_prf â† prf_key_gen;
   k_upf :: 'upf_key â† upf_key_gen;
   return_spmf (k_prf, k_upf)
 }"

lemma lossless_key_gen [simp]: "lossless_spmf key_gen"
  by(simp add: key_gen_def prf_key_gen_lossless upf_key_gen_lossless)

fun encrypt :: "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) â‡’ bitstring â‡’ 'hash cipher_text spmf"
where
  "encrypt (k_prf, k_upf) m = do {
    x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
    let c = prf_fun k_prf x [âŠ•] m;
    let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
    return_spmf ((x, c, t))
  }"

lemma lossless_encrypt [simp]: "lossless_spmf (encrypt k m)"
  by (cases k) (simp add: Let_def prf_domain_nonempty prf_domain_finite split: bool.split)

fun decrypt :: "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) â‡’ 'hash cipher_text â‡’ bitstring option"
where
  "decrypt (k_prf, k_upf) (x, c, t) = (
    if upf_fun k_upf (x @ c) = t âˆ§ length x = prf_dlen then
      Some (prf_fun k_prf x [âŠ•] c)
    else
      None
  )"

lemma cipher_correct:
  "âŸ¦ k âˆˆ set_spmf key_gen; length m = prf_clen âŸ§
  âŸ¹ encrypt k m â¤œ (Î»c. return_spmf (decrypt k c)) = return_spmf (Some m)"
by (cases k) (simp add: prf_domain_nonempty prf_domain_finite prf_domain_length
  prf_codomain_length key_gen_def bind_eq_return_spmf Let_def)

declare encrypt.simps[simp del]

sublocale ind_cca: ind_cca key_gen encrypt decrypt "Î»m. length m = prf_clen" .
interpretation ind_cca': ind_cca key_gen encrypt "Î» _ _. None" "Î»m. length m = prf_clen" .

definition intercept_upf_enc
  :: "'prf_key â‡’ bool â‡’ 'hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set â‡’ bitstring Ã— bitstring
  â‡’ ('hash cipher_text option Ã— ('hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set),
     bitstring + (bitstring Ã— 'hash), 'hash + unit) gpv" 
where 
  "intercept_upf_enc k b = (Î»(L, D) (m1, m0).
    (case (length m1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length m0 = prf_clen) of
      False â‡’ Done (None, L, D)
    | True â‡’ do {
        x â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set prf_domain);
        let c = prf_fun k x [âŠ•] (if b then m1 else m0);
        t â† Pause (Inl (x @ c)) Done;
        Done ((Some (x, c, projl t)), (insert (x, c, projl t) L, D))
      }))"

definition intercept_upf_dec
  :: "'hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set â‡’ 'hash cipher_text
  â‡’ (bitstring option Ã— ('hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set),
     bitstring + (bitstring Ã— 'hash), 'hash + unit) gpv" 
where
  "intercept_upf_dec = (Î»(L, D) (x, c, t).
    if (x, c, t) âˆˆ L âˆ¨ length x â‰  prf_dlen then Done (None, (L, D)) else do {
      Pause (Inr (x @ c, t)) Done;
      Done (None, (L, insert (x, c, t) D))
    })"

definition intercept_upf :: 
  "'prf_key â‡’ bool â‡’ 'hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set â‡’ bitstring Ã— bitstring + 'hash cipher_text
  â‡’ (('hash cipher_text option + bitstring option) Ã— ('hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set),
     bitstring + (bitstring Ã— 'hash), 'hash + unit) gpv" 
where
  "intercept_upf k b = plus_intercept (intercept_upf_enc k b) intercept_upf_dec"

lemma intercept_upf_simps [simp]:
  "intercept_upf k b (L, D) (Inr (x, c, t)) =
    (if (x, c, t) âˆˆ L âˆ¨ length x â‰  prf_dlen then Done (Inr None, (L, D)) else do {
      Pause (Inr (x @ c, t)) Done;
      Done (Inr None, (L, insert (x, c, t) D))
    })"
  "intercept_upf k b (L, D) (Inl (m1, m0)) = 
    (case (length m1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length m0 = prf_clen) of
      False â‡’ Done (Inl None, L, D)
    | True â‡’ do {
        x â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set prf_domain);
        let c = prf_fun k x [âŠ•] (if b then m1 else m0);
        t â† Pause (Inl (x @ c)) Done;
        Done (Inl (Some (x, c, projl t)), (insert (x, c, projl t) L, D))
      })"
   by(simp_all add: intercept_upf_def intercept_upf_dec_def intercept_upf_enc_def o_def map_gpv_bind_gpv gpv.map_id Let_def split!: bool.split)


lemma interaction_bounded_by_upf_enc_Inr [interaction_bound]:
  "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (intercept_upf_enc k b LD mm) 0"
unfolding intercept_upf_enc_def case_prod_app
by(interaction_bound, clarsimp simp add: SUP_constant bot_enat_def split: prod.split)

lemma interaction_bounded_by_upf_dec_Inr [interaction_bound]:
  "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (intercept_upf_dec LD c) 1"
unfolding intercept_upf_dec_def case_prod_app
by(interaction_bound, clarsimp simp add: SUP_constant split: prod.split)

lemma interaction_bounded_by_intercept_upf_Inr [interaction_bound]:
  "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (intercept_upf k b LD x) 1"
unfolding intercept_upf_def 
by interaction_bound(simp add: split_def one_enat_def SUP_le_iff split: sum.split)

lemma interaction_bounded_by_intercept_upf_Inl [interaction_bound]:
  "isl x âŸ¹ interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (intercept_upf k b LD x) 0"
unfolding intercept_upf_def case_prod_app
by interaction_bound(auto split: sum.split)

lemma lossless_intercept_upf_enc [simp]: "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (intercept_upf_enc k b LD mm)"
by(simp add: intercept_upf_enc_def split_beta prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty Let_def split: bool.split)

lemma lossless_intercept_upf_dec [simp]: "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (intercept_upf_dec LD mm)"
by(simp add: intercept_upf_dec_def split_beta)

lemma lossless_intercept_upf [simp]: "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (intercept_upf k b LD x)"
by(cases x)(simp_all add: intercept_upf_def)

lemma results_gpv_intercept_upf [simp]: "results_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (intercept_upf k b LD x) âŠ† responses_â„ (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) x Ã— UNIV"
by(cases x)(auto simp add: intercept_upf_def)

definition reduction_upf :: "(bitstring, 'hash cipher_text) ind_cca.adversary
  â‡’ (bitstring, 'hash) UPF.adversary"
where "reduction_upf ğ’œ = do {
    k â† lift_spmf prf_key_gen;
    b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
    (_, (L, D)) â† inline (intercept_upf k b) ğ’œ ({}, {});
    Done () }"

lemma lossless_reduction_upf [simp]: 
  "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ âŸ¹ lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (reduction_upf ğ’œ)"
by(auto simp add: reduction_upf_def prf_key_gen_lossless intro: lossless_inline del: subsetI)

context includes lifting_syntax begin

lemma round_1:
  assumes "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ"
  shows "Â¦spmf (ind_cca.game ğ’œ) True - spmf (ind_cca'.game ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ â‰¤ UPF.advantage (reduction_upf ğ’œ)" 
proof -
  define oracle_decrypt0' where "oracle_decrypt0' â‰¡ (Î»key (bad, L) (x', c', t'). return_spmf (
      if (x', c', t') âˆˆ L âˆ¨ length x' â‰  prf_dlen then (None, (bad, L))
      else (decrypt key (x', c', t'), (bad âˆ¨ upf_fun (snd key) (x' @ c') = t', L))))"
  have oracle_decrypt0'_simps:
    "oracle_decrypt0' key (bad, L) (x', c', t') = return_spmf (
       if (x', c', t') âˆˆ L âˆ¨ length x' â‰  prf_dlen then (None, (bad, L))
       else (decrypt key (x', c', t'), (bad âˆ¨ upf_fun (snd key) (x' @ c') = t', L)))"
    for key L bad x' c' t' by(simp add: oracle_decrypt0'_def)
  have lossless_oracle_decrypt0' [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_decrypt0' k Lbad c)" for k Lbad c
    by(simp add: oracle_decrypt0'_def split_def)
  have callee_invariant_oracle_decrypt0' [simp]: "callee_invariant (oracle_decrypt0' k) fst" for k
    by (unfold_locales) (auto simp add: oracle_decrypt0'_def split: if_split_asm)

  define oracle_decrypt1'
    where "oracle_decrypt1' = (Î»(key :: 'prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) (bad, L) (x', c', t'). 
      return_spmf (None :: bitstring option,
        (bad âˆ¨ upf_fun (snd key) (x' @ c') = t' âˆ§ (x', c', t') âˆ‰ L âˆ§ length x' = prf_dlen), L))"
  have oracle_decrypt1'_simps:
    "oracle_decrypt1' key (bad, L) (x', c', t') = 
    return_spmf (None, 
      (bad âˆ¨ upf_fun (snd key) (x' @ c') = t' âˆ§ (x', c', t') âˆ‰ L âˆ§ length x' = prf_dlen, L))"
    for key L bad x' c' t' by(simp add: oracle_decrypt1'_def)
  have lossless_oracle_decrypt1' [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_decrypt1' k Lbad c)" for k Lbad c
    by(simp add: oracle_decrypt1'_def split_def)
  have callee_invariant_oracle_decrypt1' [simp]: "callee_invariant (oracle_decrypt1' k) fst" for k
    by (unfold_locales) (auto simp add: oracle_decrypt1'_def)

  define game01'
    where "game01' = (Î»(decrypt :: 'prf_key Ã— 'upf_key â‡’ (bitstring Ã— bitstring Ã— 'hash, bitstring option, bool Ã— (bitstring Ã— bitstring Ã— 'hash) set) callee) ğ’œ. do {
    key â† key_gen;
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (b', (bad', L')) â† exec_gpv (â€ (ind_cca.oracle_encrypt key b) âŠ•â‡©O decrypt key) ğ’œ (False, {});
    return_spmf (b = b', bad') })"
  let ?game0' = "game01' oracle_decrypt0'"
  let ?game1' = "game01' oracle_decrypt1'"

  have game0'_eq: "ind_cca.game ğ’œ = map_spmf fst (?game0' ğ’œ)" (is ?game0)
    and game1'_eq: "ind_cca'.game ğ’œ = map_spmf fst (?game1' ğ’œ)" (is ?game1)
  proof -
    let ?S = "rel_prod2 (=)"
    define initial where "initial = (False, {} :: 'hash cipher_text set)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "?S {} initial" by(simp add: initial_def)

    have [transfer_rule]: 
      "((=) ===> ?S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) ?S))
       ind_cca.oracle_decrypt oracle_decrypt0'"
      unfolding ind_cca.oracle_decrypt_def[abs_def] oracle_decrypt0'_def[abs_def]
      by(simp add: rel_spmf_return_spmf1 rel_fun_def)

    have [transfer_rule]: 
      "((=) ===> ?S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) ?S))
       ind_cca'.oracle_decrypt oracle_decrypt1'"
      unfolding ind_cca'.oracle_decrypt_def[abs_def] oracle_decrypt1'_def[abs_def]
      by (simp add: rel_spmf_return_spmf1 rel_fun_def)

    note [transfer_rule] = extend_state_oracle_transfer
    show ?game0 ?game1 unfolding game01'_def ind_cca.game_def ind_cca'.game_def initial_def[symmetric]
      by (simp_all add: map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def) transfer_prover+
  qed

  have *: "rel_spmf (Î»(b'1, (bad1, L1)) (b'2, (bad2, L2)). bad1 = bad2 âˆ§ (Â¬ bad2 âŸ¶ b'1 = b'2))
         (exec_gpv (â€ (ind_cca.oracle_encrypt k b) âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt1' k) ğ’œ (False, {}))
         (exec_gpv (â€ (ind_cca.oracle_encrypt k b) âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt0' k) ğ’œ (False, {}))"
    for k b
    by (cases k; rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim_bad[where X="(=)" and ?bad1.0=fst and ?bad2.0=fst and â„ = "â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full"])
       (auto intro: rel_spmf_reflI callee_invariant_extend_state_oracle_const' simp add: spmf_rel_map1 spmf_rel_map2 oracle_decrypt0'_simps oracle_decrypt1'_simps assms split: plus_oracle_split)
    â€• â€¹We cannot get rid of the losslessness assumption on @{term ğ’œ} in this step, because if it 
      were not, then the bad event might still occur, but the adversary does not terminate in
      the case of @{term "?game1'"}. Thus, the reduction does not terminate either, but it cannot
      detect whether the bad event has happened. So the advantage in the UPF game could be lower than
      the probability of the bad event, if the adversary is not lossless.â€º
  have "Â¦measure (measure_spmf (?game1' ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} - measure (measure_spmf (?game0' ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b}Â¦ 
     â‰¤ measure (measure_spmf (?game1' ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad}"
    by (rule fundamental_lemma[where ?bad2.0=snd])(auto intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_bindI[OF *] simp add: game01'_def)
  also have "â€¦ = spmf (map_spmf snd (?game1' ğ’œ)) True"
    by (simp add: spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf split_def vimage_def)
  also have "map_spmf snd (?game1' ğ’œ) = UPF.game (reduction_upf ğ’œ)"
  proof -
    note [split del] = if_split
    have "map_spmf (Î»x. fst (snd x)) (exec_gpv (â€ (ind_cca.oracle_encrypt (k_prf, k_upf) b) âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt1' (k_prf, k_upf)) ğ’œ (False, {})) = 
        map_spmf (Î»x. fst (snd x)) (exec_gpv (UPF.oracle k_upf) (inline (intercept_upf k_prf b) ğ’œ ({}, {})) (False, {}))"
      (is "map_spmf ?fl ?lhs = map_spmf ?fr ?rhs" is "map_spmf _ (exec_gpv ?oracle_normal _ ?init_normal) = _")
      for k_prf k_upf b
    proof(rule map_spmf_eq_map_spmfI)
      define oracle_intercept
        where [simp]: "oracle_intercept = (Î»(s', s) y. map_spmf (Î»((x, s'), s). (x, s', s))
         (exec_gpv (UPF.oracle k_upf) (intercept_upf k_prf b s' y) s))"
      let ?I = "(Î»((L, D), (flg, Li)).
          (âˆ€(x, c, t) âˆˆ L. upf_fun k_upf (x @ c) = t âˆ§ length x = prf_dlen) âˆ§
          (âˆ€eâˆˆLi. âˆƒ(x,c,_) âˆˆ L. e = x @ c) âˆ§
          ((âˆƒ(x, c, t) âˆˆ D. upf_fun k_upf (x @ c) = t) âŸ· flg))"
      interpret callee_invariant_on oracle_intercept "?I" â„_full
        apply(unfold_locales)
        subgoal for s x y s'
          apply(cases s; cases s'; cases x)
           apply(clarsimp simp add: set_spmf_of_set_finite[OF prf_domain_finite]
                UPF.oracle_hash_def prf_domain_length exec_gpv_bind Let_def split: bool.splits)
          apply(force simp add: exec_gpv_bind UPF.oracle_flag_def split: if_split_asm)
          done
        subgoal by simp
        done
      
      define S :: "bool Ã— 'hash cipher_text set â‡’ ('hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set) Ã—  bool Ã— bitstring set â‡’ bool"
        where "S = (Î»(bad, L1) ((L2, D), _). bad = (âˆƒ(x, c, t)âˆˆD. upf_fun k_upf (x @ c) = t) âˆ§ L1 = L2) â†¿ (Î»_. True) âŠ— ?I"
      define initial :: "('hash cipher_text set Ã— 'hash cipher_text set) Ã—  bool Ã— bitstring set"
        where "initial = (({}, {}), (False, {}))"
      have [transfer_rule]: "S ?init_normal initial" by(simp add: S_def initial_def)
      have [transfer_rule]: "(S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S)) ?oracle_normal oracle_intercept"
        unfolding S_def
        by(rule callee_invariant_restrict_relp, unfold_locales)
          (auto simp add: rel_fun_def bind_spmf_of_set prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty bind_spmf_pmf_assoc bind_assoc_pmf bind_return_pmf spmf_rel_map exec_gpv_bind Let_def ind_cca.oracle_encrypt_def oracle_decrypt1'_def encrypt.simps UPF.oracle_hash_def UPF.oracle_flag_def bind_map_spmf o_def split: plus_oracle_split bool.split if_split intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_pmf_bind_reflI)
      have "rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S) ?lhs (exec_gpv oracle_intercept ğ’œ initial)"
        by(transfer_prover)
      then show "rel_spmf (Î»x y. ?fl x = ?fr y) ?lhs ?rhs"
        by(auto simp add: S_def exec_gpv_inline spmf_rel_map initial_def elim: rel_spmf_mono)
    qed
    then show ?thesis including monad_normalisation
      by(auto simp add: reduction_upf_def UPF.game_def game01'_def key_gen_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf split_def exec_gpv_bind intro!: bind_spmf_cong[OF refl])
  qed
  finally show ?thesis using game0'_eq game1'_eq 
    by (auto simp add: spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def fst_def UPF.advantage_def)
qed


definition oracle_encrypt2 :: 
  "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) â‡’ bool â‡’ (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict â‡’ bitstring Ã— bitstring 
    â‡’ ('hash cipher_text option Ã— (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict) spmf"
where
  "oracle_encrypt2 = (Î»(k_prf, k_upf) b D (msg1, msg0). (case (length msg1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length msg0 = prf_clen) of
      False â‡’ return_spmf (None, D)
    | True â‡’ do {
        x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
        P â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV prf_clen);
        let p = (case D x of Some r â‡’ r | None â‡’ P);
        let c = p [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg0);
        let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
        return_spmf (Some (x, c, t), D(x â†¦ p)) 
      }))"

definition oracle_decrypt2:: "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) â‡’ ('hash cipher_text, bitstring option, 'state) callee"
where "oracle_decrypt2 = (Î»key D cipher. return_spmf (None, D))"

lemma lossless_oracle_decrypt2 [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_decrypt2 k Dbad c)"
  by(simp add: oracle_decrypt2_def split_def)

lemma callee_invariant_oracle_decrypt2 [simp]: "callee_invariant (oracle_decrypt2 key) fst"
  by (unfold_locales) (auto simp add: oracle_decrypt2_def split: if_split_asm)

lemma oracle_decrypt2_parametric [transfer_rule]:
  "(rel_prod P U ===> S ===> rel_prod (=) (rel_prod (=) H) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S))
   oracle_decrypt2 oracle_decrypt2"
  unfolding oracle_decrypt2_def split_def relator_eq[symmetric] by transfer_prover

definition game2 :: "(bitstring, 'hash cipher_text) ind_cca.adversary â‡’ bool spmf" 
where 
  "game2 ğ’œ â‰¡ do {
    key â† key_gen;
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (b', D) â† exec_gpv 
      (oracle_encrypt2 key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ Map_empty;
    return_spmf (b = b')
  }"

fun intercept_prf :: 
  "'upf_key â‡’ bool â‡’ unit â‡’ (bitstring Ã— bitstring) + 'hash cipher_text
  â‡’ (('hash cipher_text option + bitstring option) Ã— unit, bitstring, bitstring) gpv" 
where
  "intercept_prf _ _ _ (Inr _) = Done (Inr None, ())"
| "intercept_prf k b _ (Inl (m1, m0)) = (case (length m1) = prf_clen âˆ§ (length m0) = prf_clen of
      False â‡’ Done (Inl None, ())
    | True â‡’ do {
        x â† lift_spmf (spmf_of_set prf_domain);
        p â† Pause x Done;
        let c = p [âŠ•] (if b then m1 else m0);
        let t = upf_fun k (x @ c);
        Done (Inl (Some (x, c, t)), ())
      })"

definition reduction_prf
  :: "(bitstring, 'hash cipher_text) ind_cca.adversary â‡’ (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.adversary"
where 
 "reduction_prf ğ’œ = do {
   k â† lift_spmf upf_key_gen;
   b â† lift_spmf coin_spmf;
   (b', _) â† inline (intercept_prf k b) ğ’œ ();
   Done (b' = b)
 }"

lemma round_2: "Â¦spmf (ind_cca'.game ğ’œ) True - spmf (game2 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ = PRF.advantage (reduction_prf ğ’œ)" 
proof -
  define oracle_encrypt1''
    where "oracle_encrypt1'' = (Î»(k_prf, k_upf) b (_ :: unit) (msg1, msg0). 
      case length msg1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length msg0 = prf_clen of
        False â‡’ return_spmf (None, ())
      | True â‡’ do {
          x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
          let p = prf_fun k_prf x;
          let c = p [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg0);
          let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
          return_spmf (Some (x, c, t), ())})"
  define game1'' where "game1'' = do {
    key â† key_gen;
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (b', D) â† exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt1'' key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ ();
    return_spmf (b = b')}"

  have "ind_cca'.game ğ’œ = game1''"
  proof -
    define S where "S = (Î»(L :: 'hash cipher_text set) (D :: unit). True)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "S {} ()" by (simp add: S_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: 
      "((=) ===> (=) ===> S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S))
       ind_cca'.oracle_encrypt oracle_encrypt1''"
      unfolding ind_cca'.oracle_encrypt_def[abs_def] oracle_encrypt1''_def[abs_def]
      by (auto simp add: rel_fun_def Let_def S_def encrypt.simps prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty intro: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_pmf_bind_reflI split: bool.split)
    have [transfer_rule]:
      "((=) ===> S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S)) 
       ind_cca'.oracle_decrypt oracle_decrypt2"
      unfolding ind_cca'.oracle_decrypt_def[abs_def] oracle_decrypt2_def[abs_def]
      by(auto simp add: rel_fun_def)
    show ?thesis unfolding ind_cca'.game_def game1''_def by transfer_prover
  qed

  also have "â€¦ = PRF.game_0 (reduction_prf ğ’œ)"
  proof -
    { fix k_prf k_upf b
      define oracle_normal
        where "oracle_normal = oracle_encrypt1'' (k_prf, k_upf) b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 (k_prf, k_upf)"
      define oracle_intercept
        where "oracle_intercept = (Î»(s', s :: unit) y. map_spmf (Î»((x, s'), s). (x, s', s)) (exec_gpv (PRF.prf_oracle k_prf) (intercept_prf k_upf b s' y) ()))"
      define initial where "initial = ()"
      define S where "S = (Î»(s2 :: unit, _ :: unit) (s1 :: unit). True)"
      have [transfer_rule]: "S ((), ()) initial" by(simp add: S_def initial_def)
      have [transfer_rule]: "(S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S)) oracle_intercept oracle_normal"
        unfolding oracle_normal_def oracle_intercept_def
        by(auto split: bool.split plus_oracle_split simp add: S_def rel_fun_def exec_gpv_bind PRF.prf_oracle_def oracle_encrypt1''_def Let_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf oracle_decrypt2_def intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_reflI)
      have "map_spmf (Î»x. b = fst x) (exec_gpv oracle_normal ğ’œ initial) =
        map_spmf (Î»x. b = fst (fst x)) (exec_gpv (PRF.prf_oracle k_prf) (inline (intercept_prf k_upf b) ğ’œ ()) ())"
        by(transfer fixing: b ğ’œ prf_fun k_prf prf_domain prf_clen upf_fun k_upf)
          (auto simp add: map_spmf_eq_map_spmf_iff exec_gpv_inline spmf_rel_map oracle_intercept_def split_def intro: rel_spmf_reflI) }
    then show ?thesis unfolding game1''_def PRF.game_0_def key_gen_def reduction_prf_def
      by (auto simp add: exec_gpv_bind_lift_spmf exec_gpv_bind map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf split_def eq_commute intro!: bind_spmf_cong[OF refl])
  qed
  also have "game2 ğ’œ = PRF.game_1 (reduction_prf ğ’œ)"
  proof -
    note [split del] = if_split
    { fix k_upf b k_prf
      define oracle2
        where "oracle2 = oracle_encrypt2 (k_prf, k_upf) b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 (k_prf, k_upf)"
      define oracle_intercept
        where "oracle_intercept = (Î»(s', s) y. map_spmf (Î»((x, s'), s). (x, s', s)) (exec_gpv PRF.random_oracle (intercept_prf k_upf b s' y) s))"
      define S
        where "S = (Î»(s2 :: unit, s2') (s1 :: (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict). s2' = s1)"

      have [transfer_rule]: "S ((), Map_empty) Map_empty" by(simp add: S_def)
      have [transfer_rule]: "(S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S)) oracle_intercept oracle2"
        unfolding oracle2_def oracle_intercept_def
        by(auto split: bool.split plus_oracle_split option.split simp add: S_def rel_fun_def exec_gpv_bind PRF.random_oracle_def oracle_encrypt2_def Let_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf oracle_decrypt2_def rel_spmf_return_spmf1 fun_upd_idem intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_reflI)

      have [symmetric]: "map_spmf (Î»x. b = fst (fst x)) (exec_gpv (PRF.random_oracle) (inline (intercept_prf k_upf b) ğ’œ ()) Map.empty) = 
        map_spmf (Î»x. b = fst x) (exec_gpv oracle2 ğ’œ Map_empty)"
        by(transfer fixing: b prf_clen prf_domain upf_fun k_upf ğ’œ k_prf)
          (simp add: exec_gpv_inline map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] spmf.map_comp o_def split_def oracle_intercept_def) }
    then show ?thesis
      unfolding game2_def PRF.game_1_def key_gen_def reduction_prf_def
      by (clarsimp simp add: exec_gpv_bind_lift_spmf exec_gpv_bind map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf split_def bind_spmf_const prf_key_gen_lossless lossless_weight_spmfD eq_commute)
  qed
  ultimately show ?thesis by(simp add: PRF.advantage_def)
qed


definition oracle_encrypt3 :: 
   "('prf_key Ã— 'upf_key) â‡’ bool â‡’ (bool Ã— (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict) â‡’
    bitstring Ã— bitstring â‡’ ('hash cipher_text option Ã— (bool Ã— (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict)) spmf"
where
  "oracle_encrypt3 = (Î»(k_prf, k_upf) b (bad, D) (msg1, msg0). 
    (case (length msg1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length msg0 = prf_clen) of
      False â‡’ return_spmf (None, (bad, D))
    | True â‡’ do {
        x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
        P â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV prf_clen);
        let (p, F) = (case D x of Some r â‡’ (P, True) | None â‡’ (P, False));
        let c = p [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg0);
        let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
        return_spmf (Some (x, c, t), (bad âˆ¨ F, D(x â†¦ p))) 
      }))"

lemma lossless_oracle_encrypt3 [simp]:

  by (cases m10) (simp add: oracle_encrypt3_def prf_domain_nonempty prf_domain_finite
    split_def Let_def split: bool.splits)

lemma callee_invariant_oracle_encrypt3 [simp]: "callee_invariant (oracle_encrypt3 key b) fst"
  by (unfold_locales) (auto simp add: oracle_encrypt3_def split_def Let_def split: bool.splits)

definition game3 :: "(bitstring, 'hash cipher_text) ind_cca.adversary â‡’ (bool Ã— bool) spmf" 
where 
  "game3 ğ’œ â‰¡ do {
    key â† key_gen;
    b â† coin_spmf;
    (b', (bad, D)) â† exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt3 key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ (False, Map_empty);
    return_spmf (b = b', bad)
  }"

lemma round_3:
  assumes "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ"
  shows "Â¦measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} - spmf (game2 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ 
          â‰¤ measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad}" 
proof -
  define oracle_encrypt2'
    where "oracle_encrypt2' = (Î»(k_prf :: 'prf_key, k_upf) b (bad, D) (msg1, msg0). 
      case length msg1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length msg0 = prf_clen of
        False â‡’ return_spmf (None, (bad, D))
      | True â‡’ do {
          x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
          P â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV prf_clen);
          let (p, F) = (case D x of Some r â‡’ (r, True) | None â‡’ (P, False));
          let c = p [âŠ•] (if b then msg1 else msg0);
          let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
          return_spmf (Some (x, c, t), (bad âˆ¨ F, D(x â†¦ p))) 
        })"

  have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_encrypt2' key b D msg10) " for key b D msg10
    by (cases msg10) (simp add: oracle_encrypt2'_def prf_domain_nonempty prf_domain_finite
      split_def Let_def split: bool.split)
  have [simp]: "callee_invariant (oracle_encrypt2' key b) fst" for key b
    by (unfold_locales) (auto simp add: oracle_encrypt2'_def split_def Let_def split: bool.splits)

  define game2'
    where "game2' = (Î»ğ’œ. do {
      key â† key_gen;
      b â† coin_spmf;
      (b', (bad, D)) â† exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt2' key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ (False, Map_empty);
      return_spmf (b = b', bad)})"

  have game2'_eq: "game2 ğ’œ = map_spmf fst (game2' ğ’œ)"
  proof -
    define S where "S = (Î»(D1 :: (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict) (bad :: bool, D2). D1 = D2)"
    have [transfer_rule, simp]: "S Map_empty (b, Map_empty)" for b by (simp add: S_def)
  
    have [transfer_rule]: "((=) ===> (=) ===> S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S))
      oracle_encrypt2 oracle_encrypt2'"
      unfolding oracle_encrypt2_def[abs_def] oracle_encrypt2'_def[abs_def]
      by (auto simp add: rel_fun_def Let_def split_def S_def
           intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI split: bool.split option.split)
    have [transfer_rule]: "((=) ===> S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S)) 
      oracle_decrypt2 oracle_decrypt2"
      by(auto simp add: rel_fun_def oracle_decrypt2_def)

    show ?thesis unfolding game2_def game2'_def
      by (simp add: map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def Map_empty_def[symmetric] del: Map_empty_def)
         transfer_prover
  qed
  moreover have *: "rel_spmf (Î»(b'1, bad1, L1) (b'2, bad2, L2). (bad1 âŸ· bad2) âˆ§ (Â¬ bad2 âŸ¶ b'1 âŸ· b'2))
    (exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt3 key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ (False, Map_empty))
    (exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt2' key b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ (False, Map_empty))"
    for key b
    apply(rule exec_gpv_oracle_bisim_bad[where X="(=)" and X_bad = "Î»_ _. True" and ?bad1.0=fst and ?bad2.0=fst and â„="â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full"])
    apply(simp_all add: assms)
    apply(auto simp add: assms spmf_rel_map Let_def oracle_encrypt2'_def oracle_encrypt3_def split: plus_oracle_split prod.split bool.split option.split intro!: rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_reflI)
    done
  have "Â¦measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} - measure (measure_spmf (game2' ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b}Â¦ â‰¤
    measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad}"
    unfolding game2'_def game3_def
    by(rule fundamental_lemma[where ?bad2.0=snd])(intro rel_spmf_bind_reflI rel_spmf_bindI[OF *]; clarsimp)
  ultimately show ?thesis by(simp add: spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def fst_def)
qed

lemma round_4:
  assumes "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ"
  shows "map_spmf fst (game3 ğ’œ) = coin_spmf" 
proof -
  define oracle_encrypt4
    where "oracle_encrypt4 = (Î»(k_prf :: 'prf_key, k_upf) (s :: unit) (msg1 :: bitstring, msg0 :: bitstring).
      case length msg1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length msg0 = prf_clen of
        False â‡’ return_spmf (None, s)
      | True â‡’ do {
          x â† spmf_of_set prf_domain;
          P â† spmf_of_set (nlists UNIV prf_clen);
          let c = P;
          let t = upf_fun k_upf (x @ c);
          return_spmf (Some (x, c, t), s) })"

  have [simp]: "lossless_spmf (oracle_encrypt4 k s msg10)" for k s msg10 
    by (cases msg10) (simp add: oracle_encrypt4_def prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty
      split_def Let_def split: bool.splits)

  define game4 where "game4 = (Î»ğ’œ. do {
    key â† key_gen;
    (b', _) â† exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt4 key âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 key) ğ’œ ();
    map_spmf ((=) b') coin_spmf})"

  have "map_spmf fst (game3 ğ’œ) = game4 ğ’œ"
  proof -
    note [split del] = if_split
    define S where "S = (Î»(_ :: unit) (_ :: bool Ã— (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict). True)"
    define initial3 where "initial3 = (False, Map.empty :: (bitstring, bitstring) PRF.dict)"
    have [transfer_rule]: "S () initial3" by(simp add: S_def)
    have [transfer_rule]: "((=) ===> (=) ===> S ===> (=) ===> rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S))
       (Î»key b. oracle_encrypt4 key) oracle_encrypt3"
    proof(intro rel_funI; hypsubst)
      fix key unit msg10 b Dbad
      have "map_spmf fst (oracle_encrypt4 key () msg10) = map_spmf fst (oracle_encrypt3 key b Dbad msg10)"
        unfolding oracle_encrypt3_def oracle_encrypt4_def
        apply (clarsimp simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf Let_def split: bool.split prod.split; rule conjI; clarsimp)
        apply (rewrite in "âŒ‘ = _" one_time_pad[symmetric, where xs="if b then fst msg10 else snd msg10"])
         apply(simp split: if_split)
        apply(simp add: bind_map_spmf o_def option.case_distrib case_option_collapse xor_list_commute split_def cong del: option.case_cong_weak if_weak_cong)
        done
      then show "rel_spmf (rel_prod (=) S) (oracle_encrypt4 key unit msg10) (oracle_encrypt3 key b Dbad msg10)"
        by(auto simp add: spmf_rel_eq[symmetric] spmf_rel_map S_def elim: rel_spmf_mono)
    qed

    show ?thesis
      unfolding game3_def game4_def including monad_normalisation
      by (simp add: map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf initial3_def[symmetric] eq_commute)
         transfer_prover
  qed
  also have "â€¦ = coin_spmf"
    by(simp add: map_eq_const_coin_spmf game4_def bind_spmf_const split_def lossless_exec_gpv[OF assms] lossless_weight_spmfD)
  finally  show ?thesis .
qed

lemma game3_bad:
  assumes "interaction_bounded_by isl ğ’œ q"
  shows "measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad} â‰¤ q / card prf_domain * q"
proof -
  have "measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad} = spmf (map_spmf snd (game3 ğ’œ)) True"
    by (simp add: spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def snd_def)
  also
  have "spmf (map_spmf (fst âˆ˜ snd) (exec_gpv (oracle_encrypt3 k b âŠ•â‡©O oracle_decrypt2 k) ğ’œ (False, Map.empty))) True â‰¤ q / card prf_domain * q"
    (is "spmf (map_spmf _ (exec_gpv ?oracle _ _)) _ â‰¤  _")
    if k: "k âˆˆ set_spmf key_gen" for k b
  proof(rule callee_invariant_on.interaction_bounded_by'_exec_gpv_bad_count)
    obtain k_prf k_upf where k: "k = (k_prf, k_upf)" by(cases k)
    let ?I = "Î»(bad, D). finite (dom D) âˆ§ dom D âŠ† prf_domain"
    have "callee_invariant (oracle_encrypt3 k b) ?I"
      by unfold_locales(clarsimp simp add: prf_domain_finite oracle_encrypt3_def Let_def split_def split: bool.splits)+
    moreover have "callee_invariant (oracle_decrypt2 k) ?I"
      by unfold_locales (clarsimp simp add: prf_domain_finite oracle_decrypt2_def)+
    ultimately show "callee_invariant ?oracle ?I" by simp

    let ?count = "Î»(bad, D). card (dom D)"
    show "â‹€s x y s'. âŸ¦ (y, s') âˆˆ set_spmf (?oracle s x); ?I s; isl x âŸ§ âŸ¹ ?count s' â‰¤ Suc (?count s)"
      by(clarsimp simp add: isl_def oracle_encrypt3_def split_def Let_def card_insert_if split: bool.splits)
    show "âŸ¦ (y, s') âˆˆ set_spmf (?oracle s x); ?I s; Â¬ isl x âŸ§ âŸ¹ ?count s' â‰¤ ?count s" for s x y s'
      by(cases x)(simp_all add: oracle_decrypt2_def)
    show "spmf (map_spmf (fst âˆ˜ snd) (?oracle s' x)) True â‰¤ q / card prf_domain"
      if I: "?I s'" and bad: "Â¬ fst s'" and count: "?count s' < q + ?count (False, Map.empty)" 
      and x: "isl x"
      for s' x
    proof -
      obtain bad D where s' [simp]: "s' = (bad, D)" by(cases s')
      from x obtain m1 m0 where x [simp]: "x = Inl (m1, m0)" by(auto elim: islE)
      have *: "(case D x of None â‡’ False | Some x â‡’ True) âŸ· x âˆˆ dom D" for x
        by(auto split: option.split)
      show ?thesis
      proof(cases "length m1 = prf_clen âˆ§ length m0 = prf_clen")
        case True
        with bad
        have "spmf (map_spmf (fst âˆ˜ snd) (?oracle s' x)) True = pmf (bernoulli_pmf (card (dom D âˆ© prf_domain) / card prf_domain)) True"
          by(simp add: spmf.map_comp o_def oracle_encrypt3_def k * bool.case_distrib[where h="Î»p. spmf (map_spmf _ p) _"] option.case_distrib[where h=snd] map_spmf_bind_spmf Let_def split_beta bind_spmf_const cong: bool.case_cong option.case_cong split del: if_split split: bool.split)
            (simp add: map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf[symmetric] map_mem_spmf_of_set prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty)
        also have "â€¦ = card (dom D âˆ© prf_domain) / card prf_domain"
          by(rule pmf_bernoulli_True)(auto simp add: field_simps prf_domain_finite prf_domain_nonempty card_gt_0_iff card_mono)
        also have "dom D âˆ© prf_domain = dom D" using I by auto
        also have "card (dom D) â‰¤ q" using count by simp
        finally show ?thesis by(simp add: divide_right_mono o_def)
      next
        case False
        thus ?thesis using bad 
          by(auto simp add: spmf.map_comp o_def oracle_encrypt3_def k split: bool.split)
      qed
    qed
  qed(auto split: plus_oracle_split_asm simp add: oracle_decrypt2_def assms)
  then have "spmf (map_spmf snd (game3 ğ’œ)) True â‰¤ q / card prf_domain * q"
    by(auto 4 3 simp add: game3_def map_spmf_bind_spmf o_def split_def map_spmf_conv_bind_spmf intro: spmf_bind_leI)
  finally show ?thesis .
qed


theorem security:
  assumes lossless: "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ"
  and bound: "interaction_bounded_by isl ğ’œ q"
  shows "ind_cca.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ 
    PRF.advantage (reduction_prf ğ’œ) + UPF.advantage (reduction_upf ğ’œ) +
    real q / real (card prf_domain) * real q" (is "?LHS â‰¤ _")
proof -
  have "?LHS â‰¤ Â¦spmf (ind_cca.game ğ’œ) True - spmf (ind_cca'.game ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ + Â¦spmf (ind_cca'.game ğ’œ) True - 1 / 2Â¦"
    (is "_ â‰¤ ?round1 + ?rest") using abs_triangle_ineq by(simp add: ind_cca.advantage_def)
  also have "?round1 â‰¤ UPF.advantage (reduction_upf ğ’œ)"
    using lossless by(rule round_1)
  also have "?rest â‰¤ Â¦spmf (ind_cca'.game ğ’œ) True - spmf (game2 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ + Â¦spmf (game2 ğ’œ) True - 1 / 2Â¦"
    (is "_ â‰¤ ?round2 + ?rest") using abs_triangle_ineq by simp
  also have "?round2 = PRF.advantage (reduction_prf ğ’œ)" by(rule round_2)
  also have "?rest â‰¤ Â¦measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} - spmf (game2 ğ’œ) TrueÂ¦ +
       Â¦measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} - 1 / 2Â¦" 
    (is "_ â‰¤ ?round3 + _") using abs_triangle_ineq by simp
  also have "?round3 â‰¤ measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). bad}"
    using round_3[OF lossless] .
  also have "â€¦ â‰¤ q / card prf_domain * q" using bound by(rule game3_bad)
  also have "measure (measure_spmf (game3 ğ’œ)) {(b, bad). b} = spmf coin_spmf True"
    using round_4[OF lossless, symmetric]
    by(simp add: spmf_conv_measure_spmf measure_map_spmf vimage_def fst_def)
  also have "Â¦â€¦ - 1 / 2Â¦ = 0" by(simp add: spmf_of_set)
  finally show ?thesis by(simp)
qed

theorem security1:
  assumes lossless: "lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) ğ’œ"
  assumes q: "interaction_bounded_by isl ğ’œ q"
  and q': "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) ğ’œ q'"
  shows "ind_cca.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ 
    PRF.advantage (reduction_prf ğ’œ) +
    UPF.advantage1 (guessing_many_one.reduction q' (Î»_. reduction_upf ğ’œ) ()) * q' +
    real q * real q / real (card prf_domain)"
proof -
  have "ind_cca.advantage ğ’œ â‰¤ 
    PRF.advantage (reduction_prf ğ’œ) + UPF.advantage (reduction_upf ğ’œ) +
    real q / real (card prf_domain) * real q"
    using lossless q by(rule security)
  also note q'[interaction_bound]
  have "interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (reduction_upf ğ’œ) q'"
    unfolding reduction_upf_def by(interaction_bound)(simp_all add: SUP_le_iff)
  then have "UPF.advantage (reduction_upf ğ’œ) â‰¤ UPF.advantage1 (guessing_many_one.reduction q' (Î»_. reduction_upf ğ’œ) ()) * q'"
    by(rule UPF.advantage_advantage1)
  finally show ?thesis by(simp)
qed

end

end

locale simple_cipher' = 
  fixes prf_key_gen :: "security â‡’ 'prf_key spmf"

  and prf_clen :: "security â‡’ nat"

  and upf_fun :: "security â‡’ 'upf_key â‡’ bitstring â‡’ 'hash"
  assumes simple_cipher: "â‹€Î·. simple_cipher (prf_key_gen Î·) (prf_fun Î·) (prf_domain Î·) (prf_dlen Î·) (prf_clen Î·) (upf_key_gen Î·)"

  for Î·

theorem security_asymptotic:
  fixes q q' :: "security â‡’ nat"
  assumes lossless: "â‹€Î·. lossless_gpv (â„_full âŠ•â‡©â„ â„_full) (ğ’œ Î·)"
  and bound: "â‹€Î·. interaction_bounded_by isl (ğ’œ Î·) (q Î·)"
  and bound': "â‹€Î·. interaction_bounded_by (Not âˆ˜ isl) (ğ’œ Î·) (q' Î·)"
  and [negligible_intros]:
    "polynomial q'" "polynomial q"
    "negligible (Î»Î·. PRF.advantage Î· (reduction_prf Î· (ğ’œ Î·)))"
    "negligible (Î»Î·. UPF.advantage1 Î· (guessing_many_one.reduction (q' Î·) (Î»_. reduction_upf Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) ()))"
    "negligible (Î»Î·. 1 / card (prf_domain Î·))"
  shows "negligible (Î»Î·. ind_cca.advantage Î· (ğ’œ Î·))"
proof -
  have "negligible (Î»Î·. PRF.advantage Î· (reduction_prf Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) +
    UPF.advantage1 Î· (guessing_many_one.reduction (q' Î·) (Î»_. reduction_upf Î· (ğ’œ Î·)) ()) * q' Î· +
    real (q Î·) / real (card (prf_domain Î·)) * real (q Î·))"
    by(rule negligible_intros)+
  thus ?thesis by(rule negligible_le)(simp add: security1[OF lossless bound bound'] ind_cca.advantage_nonneg)
qed

end

Theory CryptHOL_Tutorial

theory CryptHOL_Tutorial
imports CryptHOL LaTeXsugar
(* Author: Andreas Lochbihler, Digital Asset

text_raw â€¹%
\clearpage
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{A Tutorial Introduction to \CryptHOL{}}%
\begin{center}
  \normalfont
  {\huge A Tutorial Introduction to \CryptHOL{}}
  \\[1em]
  \large
  Andreas Lochbihler
  \\
  Digital Asset (Switzerland) GmbH, Zurich, Switzerland,
  \texttt{mail@andreas-lochbihler.de}
  \\[1ex]
  S. Reza Sefidgar
